Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons prendre pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN

Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

"Gwɛɛtaawo	
Dhiang -wo tiaandhe

WƆN -TAƆNG -MA ʼGÜ ʼSËËDHƐ

ʼSëëdhɛ ya -yë -kë -mëwɔn ʼgü ?

-Më ʼö -kë ʼyö bhii ü -de -wo pö ? Sëëdhɛ ʼö ya -yö -kë ü -de -wo ʼgü -mëwɔn
ʼgü, ʼyö ʼyii kë ˮKwi -wo, ˮDhima -wo, ʼGlɛɛ- -wo -nu ʼgü ?
-Ya ʼö- wo kwa -wo ʼgü bha, -yö -kë ˮdhϋ kö -ya -zɔn kwa -dhɛ -blɛɛsü ʼgü ꞊dhɛ
kwa -dega -wo ʼö -kë ꞊Danwo ʼka bha -yö ꞊bhlëë -sü ʼpö. -Wo -nu ʼö -Zlan -ya
-nu -da bha, -a ˮwɛɛ ʼbha ʼyaa ꞊bhlëë -sü kö -yö ziö- ʼka- ʼbha -ta. ʼPë ʼö -a -dhɛ
ʼdhö- -bha kö ʼkwa- kë, yö -mü ꞊dhɛ kö ʼmɛ ʼö ˮdhϋ -yö ꞊bhlëë -ya ö -de -wo
-bha kö -yö kë -tiaandhe -wo ˮwɛɛ pö -mɛ -nu "yan ʼgü "kpʋngtaa. Yö ꞊nëwɔn ʼgü, ꞊ya kë ꞊dhɛ ʼbhaa dɔ ü -de -wo -wo pö -dhɛ ʼka, kö -a -dhɛ -ya -bha kö
ʼö sü ꞊dɛɛ -bha, ʼü -ya -a draan- -sü -bha.
-A ꞊plɛ -naa -mü ꞊dhɛ -yö -ya kwa -de -wo ʼgü ˮdhϋ kö ʼwɔn -nu ʼö ʼwo -kë

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.

voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.

1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

-go ˮMaadhö ‘ö dho ‘ka Zɔnwɛɛn. ˮKidhʋng këng
do ö -kɔ plɛ waaˮkidhʋng ꞊plɛ(122 ).

-mɛ -nu ˮgbɩgbɩ ‘ö ‘wo
gun- -bha -wo -gun -kɔng
-yiisiö ö ga ˮsɔɔdhu (45).
Mɛ ‘bha -nu -wo -go
Togo, Gana.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.
Voici le reste de lʼ alphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser
pour savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous
ne voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼen
français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun
mot.
Voici le reste de lʼalphabet :

Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

"Yɩɩ -wɔn
Gɔndënë do ‘ö ꞊dua ö -dea ꞊geebë -gɔ

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser pour
savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous ne
voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼ en français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun mot.

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser
pour savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous
ne voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼen
français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun
mot.
Voici le reste de lʼalphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser
pour savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous
ne voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼen
français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun
mot.
Voici le reste de lʼalphabet :

Lʼorthographe DAN
Voici ce que nous pouvons utiliser
pour savoir lire et écrire en langue dan.
Les consonnes et les voyelles que vous
ne voyez pas ici sont les mêmes quʼen
français.
Attention:
1. c, h, j, qu et x nʼexistent pas en dan.
2. r ne se trouve jamais au début dʼun
mot.
Voici le reste de lʼalphabet :

‘Mɛ -nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘sëëdhɛ ‘ö ya- -kë, wo -mü ꞊Sai Zoziasü , "Dhɔɔgbö Zafe, ꞊Kesɩ Mɔyan Dhifɔngsü,

"Nimlʋʋ : 29 "Su : -Zroo -Kwɛ : 2009

"Su -bha ʼsëëdhɛ -mü		"Gwɛɛtaawo	

‘Wɔn yaa kë –sü ꞊ya sɔ ꞊dɛɛ -dedewo

‘Në dhebë ‘në ya, -a -kwɛ -yö kaɔng do ö ga do ‘yö dho ö dhuëë- ꞊keng- ‘yö- dhuëë bha ‘ö ‘gu dɔ- -bha.


ˮDhi -wo -yan kpö ‘në ‘ö go ‘sëëdhɛ ya, -a -bɛn zë -mɛ ˮpiʋ̈

‘Sëëdhɛ ya -yö -dho ‘pö- -mɛ -nu ꞊në- -nu ˮpiʋ̈ kpɛnngdhö. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ -a -nu ‘gbɛ -dhɛ ‘waa ꞊dhɔtrɔɔ ꞊plöödhɛ ˮsɔɔ.

Yö ꞊në- -wɔn ‘gü, ‘yö -kɔ ‘ö ‘wo dho wo ˮdhɛ kë- ‘ka- -bha, ‘yö ‘sëëdhɛ ya ‘ö- -a sɛɛnnë ‘bha pö.

-A -bɛn ‘yaa zë -sü ‘ka -wo kpö ˮgblʋ̈gblʋ̈ ‘gü.

꞊Ya ‘go mü, ‘pë ˗nu ‘ö- -nu ˗bhawɔn ‘dhö˗ ˗nu ˗bha kö -wa ˗nu kë, kö ˗kë ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ ˗sü ˗yö kë -a -nu ˗gɔ ˗kpɛawo, ‘yö ˗a ˗nu ˗dhiang zë. ˗A ˗wɔn ‘gü, ˗yö ˗së -a -nu ˗bha ‘ka kö ˗wa ˗wo pö. ˗A ‘gü ˗wɔn ˗nu ˗wo ˗mɔɔ ˗a -bha ‘ö ‘wo- dha ˮiin ‘ö ‘wo -a -nu -bha mɛ ‘bha dha.꞊Bɛdhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ˗a ˗nu ‘tɔ ˗nu ‘wo ‘sëëdhɛ ya˗ ‘gü, ˗dhioo ˗wo ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo˗ ‘gü, ‘mɛ ˗nu ‘ö ˗waa ˗nu ˗blɛɛsü ˗nu kë, ˮiin ‘ö ˗waa ˗nu ˗ya ꞊blëë ‘gü, ‘mɛ ‘kö yöö˗ pö ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ˗wo ya˗, ˗a ˗mɛ ‘yaa ‘dhö. ˗A ˗nu ˗bha ˗kë ˗tiaandhö ˗sü ‘ö bha, ‘yaa za -dɔ ‘gü ˗wɔn ‘ka ‘zü.





1) ‘Yuöö˗ ˮglɛɛn ˗ya ꞊nëng mɛ bhɛaˮ


  ꞊Ya kë ꞊dhɛ ‘yuöö˗ ˮglɛɛn ˮiin pë ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ꞊ya ꞊nëng mɛ ‘bha bhɛaˮ kö ˗a ˗bho mü ˗kɔ ˮslë ‘yaa ‘dhö, kö ˗a ˗mɛ ‘yaa ˮtɛɛ ˗dhɛ yö sië ˗së ‘ka, ‘wɔn ‘ö˗ ˗dhɛ ‘dhö ˗a ˗bha kö ‘ü ˗a kë ˗a mɛ ˗gɔ yö ꞊nɛ:
  
  ˗Blɛɛsü ‘gü, ˗bhö dɔ ˗a mɛ ꞊taama ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ö ü ˮyan ‘dhö -a -bha ‘sëëdhɛ -ta ya- ‘dhö. Ü ˗gbe ˗nu bɔ ˗a ˗gɔ; ü ˗kɔdhɛ ˗da ˮkʋʋ.
  
˗A ꞊plɛ ˗naa ʼgü, ü ˗kɔdhɛ bha ˗a ꞊nëng ˗a ‘gu ˗ta ˗a ˗bugɔ ˗gɔ ˮdhuʋ̈˗ ˗dhɛ waa˗ ˮsɩga ˗nu ꞊zinngü. Ü ˗kɔ ‘ya ‘dho bɔ˗ ˗a ˮsɩga ˗ta.

  ˗A ˗yaaga ˗naa ‘gü,˗a ‘gu bha ˗a bhloo ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘ka ‘ko ˗ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka kö ˮtɛɛ ˗yö ‘go ˗a ˗gɔ ˮsia˗ ꞊yën -yö ˗da. ˮKɛɛ ˗bhöö bhloo ˮvaandhö ‘ko ˗ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka. ‘Bha ˗a kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˮtɛɛ ˗yö ˗dho ‘go˗ ˗a ˗tong ‘gü ‘ö ‘pë ‘ö˗ bhɛaˮ bha ˗a bho mü. Ü ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ü ˗a ˗kë ˗a ˗gɔ ˮdhʋ̈ pinngpinngdhö ˮni kö ‘yaa ‘go sië ‘mü.
  
￹￹꞊Ya kë ‘zü ꞊dhɛ ‘mɛ ‘ö pë ‘ö ꞊nëng ˗a bhɛaˮ bha faan ˗ya kë ˗a ˗bha ꞊ya ziö- ‘ka ü ˗ta, kö ˮyan ˗së ‘yaa ˗a ˗gɔɔ ‘zü, ˗a ‘waannu ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ö ya ˗a ‘dhö ˮvaandhö:

˗A ˗wɔ ö ko ˗ta. ˗Bhö dɔ ˗a ˗ta ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ö ya ˗a ‘dhö. Ü ˗kɔ ꞊plɛ bha ˗a ˗wɔ ‘ko –ta, ˗a ˗bugɔ waa˗ ˮsɩga ꞊zinng ‘gü. ꞊Nëng ˗a ‘gu bha˗ ˗ta ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘ka ˮkɛɛ ˮvaandhö ˗wɔn ‘ka kö˗ ˮtɩng ˗yö ˗da. ˗A kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘ko ˗ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka ˮni kö ‘pë bha ‘yaa ‘go sië ‘mü.

2 ˮYua ‘ö mɛ ˗kë mɛ ga ˗yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ˗nu ‘gü (꞊Gla ˮkpɛa)

ˮYua ‘ö mɛ ˗kë mɛ ga ˗yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ -nu ‘gü bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö ‘yii ˗a kë ˗së, ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö˗ ˗mɛ ˮpɛɛn do ga ˗a ˗bha.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘bha˗ ˗ga ꞊dhɛ ü ga ˗yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ˗nu ˗wo ˗bhɔ ˗wɛɛndhö, ‘ö˗ ˮyi ˗nu ‘wo ˗kan ˗nu wo ˮslʋ̈ʋ̈dhö, ‘bha ‘dho ü ˗de sëë bho˗ ‘zü, ˗a ˮdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘ö ‘dhö ˗a ˗ga ‘ö ya:

˗Mlü ˮflɩɩ˗ bha, yɛɛnˮ ˮpiʋ̈ kö bhii ‘dho yi ‘gü, ‘yö ‘ü ˗a ˮsang ‘në ˗yan ˗yiisiö dan. Pë ˗bhö ‘ka ˮsang ꞊në ‘ö ‘kwa ˗wɩ ˗a ‘ka. ‘Bha ˗a dan ‘yö ‘ü˗ dɔ ˮyëë˗ ( kö kwa˗ ˗pö ‘ü ˮyi ˗sɛa꞊loo˗ ˗bha). ˮYi bha ˗yö ‘to˗ ˗bha ˮdhʋ̈ kö ˗dhɛ ˗yö ꞊kpaɔ. 

‘Bha ˗bö dhiaˮ ˮpiʋ̈ kö ‘bhii pë ‘bha ˗bhö ꞊kö, ‘yö ‘ü ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ya. ˮYi ‘dhɛ ‘ö ˗wɔ ˗mlü ˮflɩɩ˗ ˗bha ‘ö ˗kë ˮyi ˗blɛɛsü ‘ka bha, ‘yö ‘ü ˗a bho ˗a ˗bha, ‘ü ˮyi ˗dee ˮwɛɛ ‘në ‘bha ꞊loo pë ‘në ‘bha ‘‘gü, ‘ü˗ dɔ ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ta ‘ü ˗mlü ga bha, ˗a ꞊loo˗ ‘gü. ‘Bha˗ ˗ga ꞊dhɛ yöö ˗ya ˮtɛɛ ˗sü ˗bha bhoo, ‘yö ‘ü˗ bho ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ta, ‘yö ˮyi ꞊plɛ ˗naa bha ‘ü˗ bho ˗a ˗bha ‘zü, ‘yö ‘ü ˮyi ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ꞊loo˗ ˗bha, ‘ü˗ dɔ ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ta. ˗Yaa pö yöö ˗ya ˮtɛɛ ˗sü ˗bha, ‘yö ‘ü ˗a bho ‘mü, ‘ü ˮyi ‘dhɛ bha, ˗a bho˗ ˗bha. Kö ˗ya kë ˮyi ˗yaaga ˗naa ‘ka.

‘Yö ‘ü ˗a ˗dee ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ꞊loo pë do bha˗ ‘gü ‘ü ˗mlü bha ˗a ꞊loo ꞊bhaa. ˗Yaa pö yöö ˮtɛɛ, ‘yö ‘ü- bho ‘mü, ‘yö ˮyi bha ‘ü˗ bho˗ ˗bha, ‘ü ˗a ˗dee ‘bha꞊ loo˗ ˗bha, ‘ü˗ dɔ ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ta. Yöö ˮtɛɛ, ‘yö ‘ü- bho ‘mü, ‘ü ˮyi ‘dhɛ bha ˗a bho˗ ˗bha.꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö ˮyi ‘ö ‘ü ˗a ˗ziö ˗mlü ga bha, ˗a ˗bha ˮdhia ˮpiʋ̈ bha, ü ˗a ˗ziö ˗a ˗bha ‘ko ˗ta ˗yiisiö. ˗A ‘dhɛ ‘ö ˗wɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ˗dhɛ ˗yö ꞊kpaɔ bha, ˗ya ˗da mü kö ˗ya kë ˮsɔɔdhu. ꞊Ya ‘go mü ‘yö ‘ü ˗mlü ‘ö ˗ya dhëë ˮkan bha ‘ü˗ ˗bhö, ‘ü˗ ꞊gban ˗bhö. ‘Bha ü bo ˗a ˗bhö ˗sü ‘ka, kö ‘bhaa bhii pë ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗bhö ˗a ziaan ‘gü ˮdhɛdhɛ ˗yiisiö ˮpiʋ̈. 

˗A ˮsunma ˗yö ˗kë ꞊dhɛ kö ‘ü ˗a ˗bhö ˮdhɛdhɛ ˮsaaga (8) -naa ‘ka dhiaˮ ˮpiʋ̈, kö bhii ü ˮyan ‘to ‘yënng˗ ˗ya mɛ ˗gɔ ꞊zinng ‘gü ˮtʋ̈ng ‘ö ˗kë꞊mingdi ‘ka bha,꞊në ˗a ˗gɔ kö ‘ü gun ˗naa pë ˗bhö.

(Ü ˗dho ˗a kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔng ꞊plɛ ö ga ˮsaaga ˮpiʋ̈. ‘Waa ˗wlö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗ta tongtongdhö. ‘Bha˗ kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö ‘bha˗ ˮkian zë. Kö bhii ˗a zü ˗dee bho.

˗A ˗mlü ga ˮyi ˮnangglüü ˗nangglüü ‘ö yöö ˗da ü ga ˗yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ˗nu ‘gü bha, ꞊në yöö ˗dhii ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo mü, ‘ö ‘wo ü ga ‘gü ˗dhɛ ˗nu bhɔ sië bha, ˗a ˗nu bho ‘mü.

˗Dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔng ꞊plɛ ö ga ˮsaaga bha kö ‘ü˗ ˗nu yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ kö ‘bha ü ˗de dha ˗dedewo. Ü ˗dho kë˗ ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈.

꞊Bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ꞊në ‘ö ‘ü˗ ˗ga ˗naa ˗bhaa ‘gü bha.

3 Dhebë ‘ö ‘gbiöö˗ ‘ö dho˗ kë ˗kɔ ‘ö˗ ˗bha kö ˗yö ö ‘në ‘kpɔ ˗yi dɔ

˗Kɔ ‘ö dho, ö ‘në ‘kpɔ ˮtʋ̈ng dɔ˗ ‘ka yö nɛ:

Dhebë bha, ö ˗kɔ ˮzu ˗kɔ ˗to ꞊taama ˗sü ‘ö ˗a ˗kë, ˮiin ‘ö bɔ˗ ‘ka dhebë ˗nu ˗bɔ ˗dhɛ ‘gü bha, ‘ö sü ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗to ꞊taama ˗sü bha˗ ˗bha, ˗yö ˮsu ˗yaaga bho˗ ˮdhiʋ̈, ˮiin ˮkan- ˮdhiʋ̈. ꞊Ya ‘go mü kö ˗yö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˮsaɔplɛ (7) ˗zuö ˗a ˗ta.

˗A ˮsunman ˗yö ˗kë ꞊dhɛ kö ˗a ˗bha ˗kɔ ˮzu ˗sü ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗to ꞊taama ˗sü ˗yö kë ˮsu ‘ö ˗kë ˮkwi ˗a ˮsu ‘ka, ‘ö ˗kë zangvie ‘ka bha, ˗a ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔngdo (10) ‘ka, kö kwaa˗ dhong ꞊ni: zangvie ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔngdo, ꞊wa ˮsu ˗yaaga ˮkan ˮdhiʋ̈ kö ˗yö ˗dho ˗bɛ ˮsu ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ Ɔkötɔbrë ˮkwi ˗wo ‘gü bha, ˗a ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kaɔng do –bha. ꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈, ꞊wa ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˮsaɔplɛ ˗da ˗a ˗ta, kö ˗ya kë Ɔkötɔbrë ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔngdo ö ga ˮsaɔplɛ. Kö ˮtʋ̈ng ‘ö bha ˗a ˗zü ˗dhɛ bha ˗yö ˗dho ‘në ‘kpɔ˗ ‘ka. Kö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗kɔng do ö ga ˮsaɔdo, ö ga ˮsaɔplɛ, ö ga ˮsaaga waa˗ ö ga ˮsuɩsiö bha, ˗yö ˗dho ‘në ‘kpɔ ˗a do ‘ka.

꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈, kö ˗yö ˗së kö ‘mɛ ‘ö ˗a ˮpiʋ̈ ‘ö ö ‘në ‘kpɔ ˗yi dɔ, ˗yö ö ˮtʋ̈ng kë ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗tomaasü ‘ö ˮsu yö ˗a ‘ka bha, ˗a ‘gü.

4 Köng bhɛ ˮsɛɛ bha ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮgɩɩ˗ ˗mü

Dhebë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘gbiöö˗ ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗gɛn ꞊ya ˗bhla, ˗a ˗nu ˗bha꞊bɛdhɛ do ꞊nɛ:

Köng (ˮMaa ˮsɛ ‘gü ˗mɛ ˗nu ˗wo woo pë ˗dhɛ kpɛa) bhɛ ˮsɛɛ ‘ö bha, ꞊bɛdhɛ ˗së ˗dede ˗mü dhebë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘gbiöö˗ ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗gɛn ꞊ya ˗bhla, ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ‘ka. ‘Wo dho ˗a kë ˗kɔ ‘ö˗ ˗bha, yö ꞊nɛ: köng bhɛ ˮsɛɛ ‘ö bha, ˗waa ˗kun ꞊kwɛɛ˗ ˗tiantiandhe bho, ˮiin ‘zü ˗a ‘dhɛ ‘ö dho ꞊mɔɔ˗ ˗a ˗nu ꞊kwɛɛ˗ ˗tiantiandhe ‘ka, ˗waa ‘sü, ‘yo ‘wo ˗a ˗kpa ˗së ‘ka, ˗a ˮyi ‘ö bha, ‘yö ‘wo ˗a ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do ˮiin ꞊plɛ mü.

5 kwi ‘kun –yua

Kwi ‘kun bha, ˮyua kpɛnngdhö ‘yaa ˗mü. ˗Yö ˗kë ˮyua ˗nu ꞊në ˗a ˗nu ꞊keng˗. Kwi ‘kun bha, yöö ˗dede ‘ö ‘ya˗ ˗dhɛ ‘ö˗ ˗bha, yö ˗mü, ˗a ˗bha ˗da ‘gü ˗da ‘ö˗ wo ˗naa ꞊sië ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘ka ˗dedewo ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë ˗nu ˗gɔ bha, ˗a ‘ka.

꞊Ya kë ꞊dhɛ ‘mɛ ‘ö ˮyua ‘dhö˗ ˗bha kö ˮnɛnɛ ˗yö nu˗ ˗ta, ˗ka sɔ bho ˗a ˗mɛ ˗bha ˮpɛɛpɛdhö. ꞊Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, -ka sɔ ‘ö˗ ˗bha bha, ˗a gban bho ˗a ˗bha ˮpɛɛpɛdhö ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ö ‘në ‘dhö ˗wɔ ˗a ‘ka ö ‘kpee˗ ‘ka ya- ‘dhö.

˗A kë ˗sü ‘ö ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ bha˗ ‘dhö, ‘yö ˗së. ‘Ka sɔ bho ˗ a ˗bha ‘yö ˮnɛnɛ ˮbhʋ̈ ‘dhö ꞊lɔɔ.

‘Yaa ˗së kö ‘ka ˗a kë ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘dhɛ ‘ö ya˗ ‘dhö.

꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˮnɛnɛ ˗da ‘gü ꞊në ‘ö ˗da ˮyuamɛ bha˗ ˗gɔ.

꞊Ya ‘go mü ‘mɛ ˮʋʋ ‘mɛ ‘ö ˮnɛnɛ ‘ö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗bha, ˗yö ˗së kö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮyi mü, ˗yö ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu ˮyi mü.

꞊Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, ˗yö ˮyi ‘ö ꞊ya ˮtɛɛ ‘ö ꞊ya ꞊dhiëë bha, ˗a mü. 

Dhɛaˮ ‘kpɔ: 

˗Yö ˮdhʋ̈ tɛan˗ ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ‘në ˗nu ‘wa ‘dho ˮsukadhu ˗pë ˗nu ˗bhö, ꞊ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö bhiëˮ ‘në ˗nu woo gɔɔn ˗a ˗nu ‘gü ˗ee ?

˗A ˗yɔɔ: ꞊sua ˗mü. ˮSukadhu ˗pë ˗nu bha ‘waa bhiëˮ ‘në ˗da ‘në ˗nu ‘gü. ˮSukadhu ˗pë ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü bha, ˗yö ˗dho ˗a ˗nu gba˗ ˮsɔn kë ꞊në ˗a ‘ka. ˗A ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ ‘në ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo bha, ˗a ˗nu ꞊miëë ‘gü ˗dhɛ ‘ö ˗a ˗nu ˮsɔn ‘dhö ˗gban ˗sü ‘ka˗ ‘gü bha, ‘yii ˗kian ꞊kö. ˗A ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü bha˗ ‘gü, ‘pë ‘ö˗ ˗bha ˮnɛɛ ˗nɛɛ ˗dhɛ ‘ö ziö ˗sü ‘ka ˗naa ‘gü waa˗ pë ˮwɔ ˗sü kö ˗wa ˗nu ˗bhö, ‘në ˗nu bha ˗a ˗nu ˮsɔn ˗nu ˗wo ˗dho see˗.

꞊Ya ‘go mü, kö ‘në ˗nu ˗wo nëng kë ˮsukadhu ˗pë ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ˗bha ‘gbɛ, ˗bhöpë kpɛnngdhö ˗bhö ˗sü ˗faan ‘yaa kë ˗a ˗nu ‘gü.

˗Yö ˮdhʋ̈ tɛan˗ ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ‘yaa ˗së kö ‘në ˗nu ˗wo ˗tɔyaan ˗bhö, ꞊ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö woo kë ꞊kwan ˗mɛ ˗nu ‘ka ˗ee?

˗A ˗yɔɔ: ‘Aa bhoo, ꞊sua ˗mü. ˗A ˗dhɛ ˗ya ˗bha ˗ziaanwo kö ˗wa ˗bhö. ˗A ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ ˗tɔyaan bha ˗yö mɛ kwi ‘gü ˗dhɛ ˗bha pë ˗së ˗dede ꞊në˗ ‘ka. ˗A ˗wɔn ‘gü ‘në ˗nu ˗bhawɔn ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗wa ˗bhö.

˗Yö ˮdhʋ̈ tɛan˗ ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë ˗nu wo ꞊dhɛ dhöng˗ (seɩˮ) ˗nu, ꞊goyaa ˗nu ‘dhö bha ‘mɛ ‘ö ‘kpin˗ ˮiin kwi ‘kun ‘dhö˗ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ‘ya ‘dho ˗a ˗bhö ˗ee?

˗A ˗yɔɔ: ꞊sua ˗mü. ˗A ˗dhɛ ˗dede ˗ziaan ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈, ‘ö ˗da ‘ka ˗ziaanwo ˗a ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗bha bha, kö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ˗bhö kö ˗ya ˗nu ˮyi ˗nu mü.

6 ‘Yuöö˗ ˮglɛɛn ꞊ya ꞊nëng ü bhɛaˮ (2)

‘Ü pë ˗bhö sië kö ‘yuöö˗ ˮglɛɛn ˗yö ꞊nëng ü bhɛaˮ, ‘yuöö˗ ‘ö go ‘tɛɛ˗ ˗dede ‘ö˗ gü bha, ü ꞊wee ˗pa ‘ka kɔngga ˮiin ‘zü ‘tɛa˗ ‘gü ˗pa ‘ka kɔngga bha, ˗a ˗ma ‘tɛɛ˗ ˗dede bha ˗a ˮtʋ ˮdhiʋ̈ pinngpinngdhö. ˗Yö ˗dho ‘to ‘ka ˮdhʋ̈ ‘ö ‘yuöö˗ ˮglɛɛn bha ‘ö ꞊lɔɔ, ‘ö go ü bhɛaˮ, ‘ö ˗kë ü dhasü ‘ka.

7 ˗Bhangglöö(˗bandhe), ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ˗mü

˗Bhangglöö bhɛ ‘ö ˗ya ˗pëkë (tan) bha, ˗yö mɛ ˗gba pëbhee ‘wɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗bhö ˗dhɔ ‘ka.

‘Mɛ ˗nu ‘ö faan ‘yaa ˗a ˗nu ˗bha, ˮiin ‘ö ꞊wa kë zii , ‘ö wü waa˗ ˗tɔyaan ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ꞊ya kë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ˮgbɩɩ˗ bha, ˗a ˗dhɛ ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗wo ˗bhangglöö ˗pëkë ˗sü ˗bhö ˮtʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ‘gü.

‘Mɛ ˗nu ‘ö wü waa˗ ˗tɔyaan ˗nu bha ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗bha ˮgbɩɩ˗, ˗waa pö woo ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö, ˗wo ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗nu ˗bhö ˗bhangglöö ˗pëkë ˗sü ‘ka.

‘Mɛ ‘ö bhiëˮ ‘në ꞊ya gɔɔn ˗a ‘gü, ˗a ꞊bɛdhɛ ꞊nɛ. ˗A ˗mɛ ˗yö ˗bhangglöö ˗pëkë ˗sü ‘sü, (ˮMaa ˗mɛ ˗nu ˗wa ˗dhɛ ˗bandhe). ˗A ga ‘ö˗ ‘gü bha ˗ya bho˗ ‘gü, ˗ya ˮzu, ˗ya ‘kpɔ ‘yënng˗ ˗dhɛ. ꞊Ya ga, ‘yö ˗a ˗bi bho. ˗A ˗bi bha ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö˗ pa, ˮiin ‘ö ˗a ꞊kaan ˮbhaa ˮpuu ‘ka, ˮiin ˗mɔni ‘ka ‘ö˗ ˗bhö. 

Bhiëˮ ‘në ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ bha. ˗A ˗mɛ ˗ya ‘gü dan.

8 ‘Ü ˮta ‘sü sië kö ˗kpaa ‘në ˗yö ‘dho ü ˮyënng

˗A ‘bha ˗nu ꞊ya kë, ‘ü ˮta ‘sü sië, ˗kpaa ‘në ‘bha bha ˗yö ˗nu ‘ö ˗sɔ ü ˮyënng. ˗Yö ˗bhɔ ꞊dhɛ ˗slëë ˗yö bhɔ.

‘Bha˗ ˗ga ꞊dhɛ ꞊ya ˗sɔ ü ˮyënng, ‘bha ‘dho ü ˗kɔ ziö˗ ü ˮyan ˮdhiʋ̈. Ü slëë ‘gü ˮvaandhö kö ‘ü ü ˗ta ˗ya ziaan ‘ü ‘dho sië˗ ‘ka bha, ˗a ˗gɔ ‘kii ü ˮyan ˮpʋ. ‘Bha ˗a kë ˮdhʋ, ˗yö ˗dho ‘to˗ mü ‘ö go ü ˮyënng.

9 ‘Pë ‘ü˗ ˗bhö ‘ö ü ˮgblü ziö sië, ˗a ˮgblü ziö ‘ö bha, ˗a ꞊bɛdhɛ ꞊nɛ

  ‘Bha ‘dho ü ˗de sëë bho˗ ˮwɛɛwɛ ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮwɛɛ ‘bha mɔɔ˗ ˗sü ‘ka ꞊dhɔtrɔɔ ꞊plöö.
  
  ˗Dhɛ ˗ga, ü ˮgblü ‘ö ziö sië, ˗bhö ꞊wee ˗bi ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘sü ü kɔngga ˮiin ˮsang ‘në ˮzɔ ˮdhiʋ̈, ‘ü˗ ˗da pë ‘në ‘bha ‘gü, ‘ü ˮyi ꞊loo˗ ˗ta. ‘Bha pë ziö˗ ‘gü ꞊ya kaan˗ ˮkwëë ˗së ‘ka, ‘yö ‘ü mü. ‘Bha ü bo ˗a mü ˗sü ‘ka, ü ˮgblü ˗blɛɛsü ‘ö dho ziö˗ ˗a ziaan˗ ˗ta bha, ꞊ya ‘go ˗a ‘gü, kö ü bha ˮgblü ziö bha ꞊ya yën. ˮKö ‘zü ‘ö ‘wo˗ pö bhii ˮta ꞊gblɛɛn ‘kpɔ ꞊dhɛ mɛ ˗yö go ˮMaadhö mɛ ˗yö dho ‘Biya, ü ˮgblü ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ‘yii ‘dho ziö˗ ziaan ‘ka ‘ü dho ‘ü ꞊loo˗ ‘ka.

10 ‘Ö ü ˮpiʋ̈ ‘ü kë ü faan ‘gü ˗kpɛɛwo: ˮnimlɔɔ ˗blɛɛsü

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ ˮpiʋ̈ ‘ö kë ö faan ‘gü ˮtʋ̈ng ꞊gban ‘gü,‘ö˗ ˮpiʋ̈ ˮgʋng ‘ya ‘dho ö kë˗ ꞊plɛplɛ, dhiaˮ ˮpiʋ̈ ꞊gban ˮpɛpɛ ‘gü, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ˗bö kö ‘yii pë ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗bhö ꞊kö, ˮyi ˗dede ‘ö ya, ˗a ˗sandhe, ˮiin ‘zü ˗a ˗zuɛɛbhɛ, ˮkwi ˗yö ö bha pë ˗dhɛ ‘dhiitrë, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya do mü. Ya ö bo ˗a ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü ‘ka, ‘yö yöö pë ˗bhö, ‘yö gun ˗a ˗bhö ˗naa ꞊tɔn. ˮKɛɛ ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ö ‘gü dɔ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘ya ‘dho˗ pö ‘ö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗nu ˗da ˗a ˮyi bha ˗a mü ˗sü ꞊zinng ‘gü. ˗A ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü bha ‘yaa ˗së.
  
  ‘Wɔn ‘ö bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö˗ ˗ya ꞊bhlëë ‘gü ˗dedewo, kö ˗a ˗mɛ ꞊ya ‘wɔn ˗së kë ö ˗de ˗dhɛ.

11 ‘Ö ü ˮpiʋ̈ ‘ü kë ü faan ‘gü ˗kpɛɛwo: ˮnimlɔɔ ꞊plɛɛ ˗naa

  ˗Kɔ do ‘ö ˗kë faan ‘gü ˗sü ˮnimlɔɔ ˗blɛɛsü ˗bha ‘dhö˗ ‘ka, ‘ö ˗gban ˮyi ‘dhiitrë do mü ˗sü ˗bha bha, ‘yö ˗a ‘dhɛ ‘ö ya, ˗a ˗bha ‘dhö˗ ‘ka. ‘Bha ˗bö dhiaˮ ˮpiʋ̈ kö ‘bhii pë ‘bha ˗bhö ꞊kö, ˗bhö mɛtii dhöng˗ (seɩˮ) bhɛ do bhloo kö ‘ü ˗a ˮyi ꞊loo ˮvɛdhɛ do ‘gü, ‘ü ˮyi ꞊loo˗ ˗ta ˗yö ˮvɛdhɛ bha˗ pa. ˗A kaan˗ ˮkwëë ˗së ˗dede ‘ka. ˗A mü. ˮKɛɛ ˗a kë ˮdhʋ̈ yi ꞊gban ˮpɛpɛ ‘ka. ‘Bha˗ kë ˮdhʋ̈, ü ˗dho kë ü faan ‘gü ˮtʋ̈ng ꞊gban ‘gü, ˮgʋng ‘yii ‘dho ü kë˗ ꞊plɛplɛ.

12 ꞊Mlɛɛ ꞊ya ö ˮdhidhi -pɛn ü ˮyënng

  ꞊Mlɛɛ ꞊ya ö ˮdhidhi ꞊wɛng ü bha mɛ ‘bha ˮyënng ˗dhɛ ‘ö ˮdhɔɔkɔ ‘dhö ˗bha ˗a ‘gü, ü ‘gü dɔ ˮgbɩɩ˗ kö ‘ü ˮnɔnɔ, ‘ö ˗kë ˮkwi ˗a ˮnɔnɔ ‘ka, ‘ö ‘yaa ˮnɛɛnɛɛ, ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ˮkwi ˗wo ‘gü bɔngdhe ‘wluziö bha, ‘ü ˗a do ‘dhɔ kö ‘ü˗ ˮyi yö ‘mɛ ‘ö ꞊mlɛɛ ‘dhö ö ˮdhidhi ꞊pɛn ˗a ˮyënng bha, ˗a ˮyan ga ꞊plɛ bha ˗a ˗nu ‘gü. ‘Bha˗ kë ˮdhʋ̈, ˗yö ˗dho kë˗ ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈. ‘Wɔn ‘bha ˗bha ‘bha, ‘yii ‘dho ˗a kë˗ tongtongdhö. ꞊Bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ˗dede ꞊në ‘ü ˗a -ga sië bha.

13 ˮSɔn kë ꞊bɛdhɛ

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö ü ˮsɔn ‘dhö ü kë sië, ꞊ya kë ꞊dhɛ ü ˮsɔng ga ‘ö ü kë sië bha ˗a ˗yɛ ga ‘dhö˗ ‘gü, ‘bha ‘dho ü ˗de sëë bho˗, ꞊bɛdhɛ ‘ö ya ˗a kë.
  
  Ü ˮsɔnga bha ‘ö ü kë sië ˮtʋ̈ng ˗dede ‘ö˗ ‘ka bha, ‘bha ‘dho ‘kɔ ꞊taama kë ˗dhɛ ‘gü, yeeˮ ˮviëë ‘në ‘bha ˗yö kë ü ˗gɔ. ‘Bha˗ ‘kɔ ꞊taama bha˗ kë, ü ‘gü dɔ ˮgbɩɩ˗ kö ‘ü ü ˗dega gbo ‘ö bha, ‘ü˗ sɛɛnnë ‘bha ‘sü ˮdhü ‘në ˮzɔ ˮdhiʋ̈ kö ‘ü ˗a ˗ya ‘gü, ‘ü yeeˮ ˮviëë bha ˗a ˗ya ˗ta. Ü ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ‘ü˗ ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘ko ˗ta ꞊plɛ ˮiin ˗yaaga ˗dhɛkpaɔyi do bha˗ ‘ka. Kö ü gbo ‘ü˗ ˗ya ˗a ‘gü bha, ˗a ꞊fii ‘kö bha ˗yö ˗da ü ꞊miëë bha ˗a ˮpiʋ̈, kö ü ˮsɔn bha ˗yö dɔ dinngdhö, kö ˗ya kë ˗a bo ˗sü ꞊në ˗a ‘ka bha. ‘yii ‘dho ü kë˗ ‘zü tongtongdhö ‘ö to˗ ‘ka ˮdhʋ̈ ˗kwɛ ‘gbɛ ˗dede ˮpiʋ̈.
  
  ˗A ‘gü ma ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ü ˗dega gbo ˗mü. ˗A ˗kë ‘ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü ‘gü, ˗a ˗yënng ‘ya ‘dho ü kë˗. Mɛ ‘yaa ˗yënng kë mɛ dha ˗pë ˗gɔ.

14 ˗Dhiëë ꞊bɛdhɛ

  ‘Mɛ ‘ö ˗dhiëë ꞊ya dɔ ü ˗bha ˗dee ‘gü, ˗bhö ˗bhangglöö (˗bandhe) bhɛ ‘ö ‘yii ˗pë kë (tan), ‘ö ˗kpo ‘ka bha, ˗a ˮkplü ˮkan kö ‘ü ˗a ˗ya ü bha ˗dhiëë bha ˗a ˗ta. ˗Yö ˗dho dɔ˗ ˮvaandhö. ꞊Ya bo dɔ ˗sü ˗zë ˗a ‘ka, kö ˗a zua ˗wɔn ꞊në ‘ö ꞊ya ‘to.

15 ˗Bhangglöö ˗dhü ˮyi

˗Bhangglöö (˗bandhe) ˗dhü ˮyi bha bhiëˮ ‘në ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ˗mü.

˗A ˗dhü ˮyi bha, ˮkaflɩɩ ˗mü ‘ka ˮsang ‘në ˮiin ‘zü ˮsang ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë bha, ˗a do ‘sü kö ‘ü ˗bhangglöö ˗dhü bha, ˗a ˮyi ˗yan ˗yaaga ˮiin ˗yiisiö ‘kun ˗a ‘gü. ꞊Ya ‘go mü kö ˮsang ‘në do bha ‘ü˗ ‘sü kö ‘ü ˮzɔ ˮyɔn ˗yan ˗yaaga ˮiin ˗yiisiö dan ˗a ‘gü ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ü ˗bhangglöö ˗bha ˗kë ˗a ‘ka bha˗ ‘dhö. ‘Bha ü bo kö ‘ü ˗a ˗bhangglöö ˮyi ‘ü˗ dan bha ‘dhö , ˮzɔ ˮyɔn ‘ü˗ dan bha˗ ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu gban ꞊loo ˮkaflɩɩ ˮyi ˮwɔsü ˗dede ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do ‘gü, ‘ü pë ziö ˗a ‘gü kö ˗yö ˗kaan ˮkwëë ˗së ‘ka, kö ‘ü ˗a mü.

˗Yö ˗ziö bhiëˮ ˗gɔ ꞊dhɛ mɛ ˗yö ˗më ˗kë.

16 ˮÜü ˗dɔn ‘ö ‘në ˗nu ˗kë bha, ˗a ꞊bhɛdhɛ ꞊nɛ:

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˮüü ‘dhö ü bha ‘në kë sië, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ö ˮtʋ ‘to ˗së ‘ka kö ˗ya kë ꞊ni:

˗Yabha suu ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ai ˮiin lai (aˮ ˗i, laˮ ˗yi) bha˗ ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ˮpɛn do ˮiin ˮpɛn ꞊plɛ ‘sü. ˗Ya wüü˗ wüü˗ ˮiin ˗ya ꞊dhiëë. ˗A ˗böö bha, ˗ya ‘sü kö ˗ya ꞊loo ˮyi ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do ‘ö ˗ya ˮtɛɛ ˗tiaandhe ‘ka, ˗a ꞊bhaa. ˗A ˗mɛ ˗yö ö kwaa˗ ˗zü ˮtʋ̈ng kpö ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka. ˮKwi ˗nu ˗wo woo˗ pë ˗pö minitö ˗kɔng do. ꞊Ya ꞊dhiëë kö ˮsang ‘në sɛɛnnë bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ˗yan ꞊plɛ ˮiin ˗yaaga ꞊loo ˗bhöpë ˮiin müpë ˮnɛɛnɛɛ ‘bha ‘gü, kö ˗ya kaan˗ ‘ka, ˗ya nu ‘në ‘ö ˮüü ‘dhö ˗a kë sië bha ˗a ˗dhɛ. ˮKɛɛ ˗yö kë ‘në ‘ö ˗a ˗kwɛ ‘yii yö ꞊kö do -bha ˗a ‘ka.

17 ‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ ‘gu ꞊ya ma˗ ˗bha

‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ ‘gu ꞊ya ‘ma˗ ˗bha (‘ö ‘yaa ö gboo sië) ‘ö dho ˗a kë ˗kɔ ‘ö˗ ˗bha yö ꞊nɛ.

˗A ˗mɛ ˗yö ˗yabha kpö do ‘sü ˗ya kaan˗ kaan˗. ꞊Ya ö bo ko ˗ya ꞊loo ˮyi ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do ˮiin ꞊plɛ ‘ö ꞊ya ˮsukadhu ˗da ˗a ˗bha ˗a ꞊bhaa, ˗ya dɔ ˮsiʋ̈ʋ̈ kö ˗yö ˮtɛɛ ˮtʋ̈ng kpö ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka (minitë ˗kɔng do ˮiin ˗kɔngdo ö ga ˮsɔɔdhu ˮpiʋ̈). ꞊Ya bo ˮtɛɛ ˗sü ‘ka, ꞊ya ꞊dhiëë, dhiaˮ ˮpiʋ̈, ‘mɛ bha kö ‘yii pë ‘bha ˗bhö ꞊kö, kö ˗ya ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do mü. Yɛɛnˮ ˮpiʋ̈ kö yöö ‘dho yi ‘gü, kö ˗ya do mü. 

Kö ˗ya ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü ꞊bhlëë ˗ya, ˗a ‘gu ˗ta ˗yö ˗dho lɔɔ˗ 

ˮIin ‘zü ‘mɛ ‘ö ˗a ‘gu ꞊ya ‘ma˗ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö mɛtii seɩˮ bhɛ do ˮiin ꞊plɛ ‘sü ˗ya ˮyi bho ˗ya ꞊loo ˮyi ‘ö ‘yaa ˮwɔwɔsü ˮiin ‘ö ‘yaa ˗sɛa bha ( ‘kwa˗ pö ˮdhʋ̈ kö kwa ˗a ˗pö ˮyi ‘kpɔng˗ ˗kpɔng), ˗a ꞊bhaa. ˗Ya kaan˗ ‘ka ˗së ‘ka. ꞊Ya ö bo kö ˗ya mü. ˮKɛɛ ‘ö˗ mü sië kö ˗yö ˮta ‘sü sië- ‘ka ˮlɛɛdhö, kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö ˗yö ˗da ˗a kwi ‘gü ˗së ‘ka, ˗ya ‘gu lɔɔ.





18 ‘Mɛ ‘ö ꞊gwan ꞊ya ˮkan˗ ˗ta

‘Mɛ ‘ö ꞊gwan ꞊ya ˮkan˗ ˗ta ‘ö dho ˗a kë ˗kɔ ‘ö ˗bha kö ˗yö ˮkan ˗yö ꞊nɛ.

˗Blɛɛsü ‘gü, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˗ya ˮzɛnngdhö.

˗A plɛ ˗naa,˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ö yun bhloo minitë ˮsɔɔdhu ‘piʋ̈, ˮiin ˗yö ‘to˗ ‘ka ˮdhʋ̈ ˗a ꞊gwan ˗yö ‘gbaannu. ꞊Ya kë ‘zü ꞊dhɛ ‘yaa ˗yan sië, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö yeɩˮ ˮviëë kpö ‘në ˗nu kë kö ˗ya ˗nu ˗sɔ ö yun ˮdhi ˗nu bha ˗a ˗nu ‘gü, kö ˗ya ˗nu ˮzɔ ˗nu ‘to ˮyɛɛ˗. ꞊Ya ö bo ˗a ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü ‘ka kö ˗yö ö yun ˗nu bhloo ‘zü ‘bha wo minitë ˮsɔɔdhu ‘ka. ꞊Ya ‘go mü kö ˗ya yeɩˮ ˮviëë ˗nu bha ˗a ˗nu ‘to mü ˮdhɛdhɛ kpö ‘në ‘bha ‘ka, kö ˗yö gun ˗naa ˗a bho ‘mü ˮlɛɛdhö ö ‘suaan˗ ‘ka.

(‘Mɛ ‘ö ꞊ya kë ꞊sië ꞊sië ‘ö ꞊gwan ‘dhö ˗kan ˗a ˗ta, ˗yö nëng kë ˗nu wo seɩˮ ‘ö ˗kë ˮkwi ˗a seɩˮ ‘ka, ‘ö ‘wo ˗a ˗dhɛ orangziö bha˗ ‘dhö, ꞊tanmatii ˗nu ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ˗bha, kö ˗yö mɛtii seɩˮ ˗nu ˮyi mü.

‘Ö˗ kë sië ˮdhʋ̈, ꞊gwan ‘yii ‘dho nu˗ ˗ta.

19 Dɔn ˮkpɛa ꞊bɛdhɛ: ˮnimlɔɔ do

‘Mɛ ‘ö dɔn ˮkpɛa ‘dhö˗ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮkaflɩɩ ˗mü ‘ka ˮsang ‘në ‘sü, ˗yö ˮzɔ ˮyɔn ˗yan do dan ˗a ‘gü ˗ya ꞊loo pë ‘bha ‘gü. ˗Yö ˮsang do bha˗ ‘sü ˗yö mɛtii seɩˮ ˮyi ˮsang ‘në ˗yan do ‘dhö, ˮkwi ˗a we ˮgbɩɩ˗, ˮsang ‘në ˗yan do ‘dhö ˗yö pë ˗yaaga bha, ˗a ˗nu ꞊gban kaan˗ ˮkwëë ˗së ‘ka. ˗A ˗mɛ ꞊ya ö bo, ˮsang ‘në bha ‘yö ˗a ˗yan do mü. ˮdhɛdhɛ ˗yaaga ꞊ya ziö, ‘yö do ‘bha mü.

ˮDhɛdhɛ ˗yaaga ꞊ya ziö, ‘yö ˗a do ‘bha mü. ˗A ˗yaaga ‘bha ꞊ya ziö ‘zü, ‘yö ˗a do ˮwɛɛ ‘bha mü.

ˮKɛɛ ꞊ya kë ꞊dhɛ ‘në ‘ö ‘yɔn ˗bha ˮiin ‘mɛ ‘ö ˮyua ‘bha, ‘dhö ˗a ˗bha, ‘ö ˮyua bha ‘ö dɔn ‘dhö˗ ˮpiʋ̈, kö ‘ka ‘dho we ˮgbɩɩ˗ ‘kö bha, ˗a ˗da ˮpiʋ, ‘ö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya mü. ˗A ˮbin

꞊Bɛdhɛ ‘ö ‘ka˗ ˗ga ˗naa ˗bhaasü ‘ka bha, ꞊bɛdhɛ ˮgbɩɩ˗ ˗mü.





20 Dɔn ˮkpɛa ꞊tɔɔ ꞊bɛdhɛ

‘Mɛ ‘ö dɔn ˮkpɛa ‘dhö˗ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ꞊ya ˮyi dɔ ˮsiʋ̈ʋ̈, ꞊ya ˮtɛɛ ˗dedewo ˗së ‘ka, ‘yö ˗a ˗mɛ ‘dhö ˗a ꞊loo ˮgbʋnggbʋ ‘gü ‘ö ö ˗gɔ dun ˗a ˗ta kö ˗a ˗mɛ ꞊ya sɔ ‘ma ö ˗gɔ waa˗ ˮgbʋnggbʋ ꞊gban ˗bha. ˗Yaa kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘yö ˗a ˮdhuu bha ‘ö ˗a ˗gan ö ˮdhi waa˗ ö yun ‘gü. ‘Yö ˗a ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈, ‘ko ˗ta ‘gbɛ ‘ka ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗bha.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˗a yun ‘gü ꞊ya ta, ˗a ˗mɛ ꞊ya kë ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ do ‘ö ‘go sië ˗a ma˗ ‘ka, dɔn ˮkpɛa ˗bha ‘ka bha˗ ‘dhö.

21 ˮKwi ˗naa ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘yaa ‘mɛ ‘ö˗ ˗gɔ

˗Dhɛ ‘ö ˮkwi ˗naa ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘ö ˗kë ˮsɔn ˗zu ‘ka ˗pë ‘ka ‘yaa ˗bha, ‘ü dho ˗a kë ˗kɔ ‘ö˗ ˗bha yö ꞊nɛ. ˮDhü ‘ö ‘wo ꞊mɔɔ˗ ˗bha ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗kë ‘gbɛsɛɛ ‘ka, ˗a sɛɛnnë do ˮkan kö ˗a zü bha ‘ü˗ ˮzɔ dɔ kö ˗yö kë ˗ziö ˮsɔn ‘gü ˗pë ‘ka. ˗A ˗gɔ bha, ˗a ˮzɔ ˗bhö kö ˗a ˮsɛɛ ˗yö kë, kö ‘ü ˗a ziö ü ˮsɔn ˗bha.

22 ˗Dhɛ ‘ö ˮkwi ˗naa pë ˗böö ‘ö ‘wo wo ˮsɔn ˗zu ˗a ‘ka ‘yaa˗ ˗bha

꞊Ya kë ꞊dhɛ pë ˗böö ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗ya ˮsɔn ˗zu ‘ka ˗pë ˮdhiʋ̈ bha, ‘yaa ˗dhɛ ‘ö˗ ˗bha ˮiin ‘mɛ ‘ö˗ ˗gɔ, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ꞊wee ˗bi ‘në sɛɛnnë waa˗ ‘seng˗ -bi sɛɛnnë kaan˗ ˮkwëë ˗ya ˗ya ˮsɔn ˗zu ‘ka ˗pë ˗ta. ˮKɛɛ ˗yö ˮsɔn ˗zu ‘ka ˗pë bha, ˗a ˗dhɛ ‘ö yöö˗ ziö ö ˮsɔn ˗bha bha, ˗a ꞊tɔɔ ꞊kö ˗blɛɛsü ˮyi ‘ka kö pë ˗bi bha, ˗yö ‘ma˗ ‘gü ˗së ‘ka. ꞊Ya ‘go mü kö ˗ya ziö ö ˮsɔn ˗bha. ˗Yö ˗dho ˗a ˮsɔn ‘zu˗ ˗së ‘ka ˗dedewo.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘seng˗‘yaa ˗a ˗gɔ, ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö˗ ˗kë ꞊wee ˗bi doseng ‘ka.

23 ‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ bhɛaˮ ˗dhɛ ꞊ya ‘to ˗nɛɛsi

  ˗A ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮyi ‘në ‘bha dɔ pɛng ˮdhiʋ̈. ꞊Ya ‘kun kö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya bho ‘mü ˗yö ꞊wee ‘në ‘bha ˗da ˗a ˮpiʋ̈ ˗ya mü.

24 ‘Mɛ ‘ö ‘kpin˗ ‘dhö˗ kë sië

꞊Ya kë mɛ ‘kpii˗ ˮiin ‘në ‘kpii˗ ‘ka, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮyi ‘ö ꞊wee ‘në ‘bha ‘dhö ˗a ˗bha, ˗a ꞊loo ö ꞊kwɛɛ˗ kö ˗ya ˮgan ö yun ‘gü.

25 ‘Mɛ ‘ö yi ‘yaa ˗da sië ˗a ˮyan –bha

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˮdhʋ̈ bha, yɛɛnˮ ˮpiʋ̈, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ö ‘zu ˮyi ‘wɔɔ˗ ˗wɔɔ ‘ka. ‘Kwa˗ pö ˮdhʋ̈ kö kwa˗ pö ˮyi ‘ö ‘yaa ˮwɔsü ˮiin ‘ö ‘yaa ˗sɛa. ꞊Ya ‘go mü, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˮnɔnɔ ˮwɔwɔsü ˮvɛdhɛ ˗yan do mü kö ˗yö gun‘waannu ˗naa. ꞊Ya ‘go ‘bha wo ‘mü, ‘ö sü ‘yënng˗ ˗ya mɛ ˗gɔ ꞊zinng ‘gü ˮtʋ̈ng ˗bha ‘ö dho ‘ö yö ˗a ‘ka yɛɛnˮ ˮpiʋ̈ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ‘ya ‘dho ˮkaflɩɩ ˮiin ‘pë ‘ö ‘wo˗ ‘te˗ kë bha, ˗a ‘bha mü˗ tongtongdhö.

26 ˗Dhioo ˗nu ‘ö ‘ö ‘wo –së kwa –bha ‘ka

˗Blɛɛsü ‘gü:

‘wëëga ‘në ‘bha ꞊ya kë ‘mɛ ‘ö ˗a ˗gɔ, ‘ö˗ ˗mɛ ˮpiʋ̈ ꞊dhɛ ‘ö ö bha ‘në ˗ta ‘kun kö ˗yö kë ö faan ‘gü ˗së ‘ka ˮtʋ̈ng ꞊gban ‘gü, ˗a ˗mɛ ‘ya ‘dho we ˮnɛɛnɛɛ ‘dhɔ˗ ö bha ‘në bha˗ ˗dhɛ. 

˗A꞊plɛ ˗naa: 

˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˗tɔyaan ˗nu, ˮgwɛɛ ˗nu, ˮnɔnɔ ˗sɛa ˮiin ꞊kplü ‘kun ˗sü, ˮiin ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë ˗nu wo dhöng˗ (seɩˮ), ꞊tanmatii ˗nu, ze ˗nu, ˮkpako ˗nu, ˗bhangglöö (˗bandhe) ˗nu, ꞊vokaa ˗nu, ˮmanggloo ˗nu, glɔɔ ˮnɛɛnɛɛ ˗nu ‘ö ˗da ˗a ‘ka ˗a ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗bha bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ‘dhɔ ö bha ‘në ˗dhɛ ˮtʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ‘gü.

˗A ˗yaaga ˗naa: 

dhebë ‘ö ‘në ˗dee ‘ö˗ ˗gɔ ˮyɔn ˗bha, ‘pë ˗nu ‘ö ‘kwa go ˗a ˗nu ‘tɔ ma˗ bha, ˗a dhebë ‘ö ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗ya ˗nu ˗bhö ˮtʋ̈ng ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ‘gü, kë ˮdhʋ̈ kö ˗yö ˗da ˗a ‘yɔn ‘gü ˗së ‘ka, kö ˗yö kaan˗ ˗a ˮyɔn ˮyi ‘ka, kö ‘në ˗yaa mü,˗yö kë ö faan ‘gü ˗së ˗dede ‘ka.

˗A ˗yiisiö ˗naa: 

baa ‘ö ˗kë ˗bhö ˗baa ‘ka bha, ˗a ˮdhɛ bha, ˗kwa nëng kë ˗a ˗bhö ˗sü ˗bha. ˗Bhöpë ˗së ˗dede ˗mü. ˗Yö mɛ ˗da mɛ faan ‘gü. Kwa ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ‘kwa ˗a ꞊flügüdhe ˗kë ‘pö.꞊Ya ‘go mü, ˮwɩsɩ ˮdhɛ ˗nu, ze ˮdhɛ ˗nu, kplɔɔˮ ˮdhɛ ˗nu waa˗ ˮkwi ˗a ze ˮdhɛ ˗nu ‘wo bha, kwa ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ‘ö ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ˮkpɛa kpɔ ‘ö ‘kwa˗ ˗nu ˗bi bho ‘dodo ‘ka, ‘ö ‘kwa˗ ˗nu ꞊kaan –dee ‘në ˗nu ˗bha ˮbhaa ˮyi ‘ka. ˗Yö ‘në ˗nu ˗da faan ‘gü.

27 ˮSɛɛ ˗slëë

˗A ˗dhɛ ˗ya ˗bha kö ‘kwa ˮsɛɛ ˗slëë ˗da ꞊sië ꞊sië kwaa˗ ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘gü, ‘kwa˗ ˗nu ˗bhö ‘ka,. ˗A kë ‘ö ‘kwa dho wo˗ ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗a ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ ꞊ya kë ˮdhʋ̈, ˗yö ˗dho kwa gba˗ pë ˗bhö ˗dhɔ ˗nu ‘ka, ‘ö ‘nii˗ ˗da kwa ‘gü.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˗a ˮpiʋ̈ ‘zü ‘ö kë ˮtan bho ˗mɛ ‘ka, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ˮsɛɛ ˗slëë bha ˗a ˗bhö ˮzɔ ˮyɔn ‘ka ˮiin ˮsukadhu ‘ka. ‘Mɛ ‘ö ˗yaa kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘ko ˗ta ‘gbɛ ꞊sië ꞊sië, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗wo ˗yö ˗dho dhi˗ ꞊dhɛ ˗maa ‘në ‘bha ‘ö ˮtan bho˗ ˗naa ˗dhɛkpaɔ ˮdhiʋ̈ ‘ö ˗a ˗wo ‘dhö ˗së bha, ˗a ‘dhö.

28 ˗Bhöpë ‘bha ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ˮkwi ˗wo ‘gü karɔtö, ˗a kë ˗yë

˗Blɛɛsü ‘gü,

karɔtë bha, dhebë ‘ö ‘gbiöö˗ kö ˗ya ꞊dhiëë, ˗ya ˮyi bho, kö ˮtʋ̈ng ‘ö˗ ‘ka ‘gbiöö˗ bha ˗yö nëng kë ˗a ˮyi mü ˗sü ˗bha, ˗a ‘në ‘kpɔ ˗sü ‘yaa ꞊gbɔɔn, ‘yaa kë ˮgbɩɩ˗.

˗A ꞊plɛ ˗naa,

‘në ‘ö ˗a ˮgblü ‘dhö ziö sië ˗yaa ˮyi mü, ˗a ˗bha ˮgblü ziö ˗yö ˗yën.

˗A ˗yaaga ˗naa,

‘mɛ ‘ö ˗a ga ˗yö ‘ko ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ˗nu ꞊wa ‘to ˗nɛɛsü, ꞊ya nëng kë ˗a ˮyi mü ˗sü ˗b̄ha, ˗yö ˗kë ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈.

˗A ˗yiisiö ˗naa,

‘mɛ ‘ö nëng ˗kë ˗a ˮyi mü ˗sü bha, ‘yaa kë zii ˮvaandhö. ˗A ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ pë ‘bha -nu -wo kwa ꞊yɔɔn ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo ˮslë ꞊mɔɔ- -bha kö -wo kwa kë zii; kɔrɔtë ˮyi bha -yö -ziö -a ˗nu ˗gɔ zë -sü -gɔ.

29 ˗Më ‘ö ‘kwa dho ˗a ˗bhö kö ˗kë ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈sü ˗yö kë kwa ˗gɔ. ˮYua ˗nu ‘ö ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘waa ˗tiaandhe ‘wo˗ nu mɛ ˗dhɛ

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˮdhʋ̈ dodo ‘ka, ˗a ˗bhawɔn ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗yö pëbhee ˗së ˗bhö, kö ˗yö ˗ba ˗tiaandhe ‘ka, ˗yö kë ö faan ‘gü, ˗yö yë kë ˗dedewo ö kë ˗kɔ ˗ta ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ‘gü ˗kpɛawo.

ˮYua ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ˗wo mü ꞊dɛɛ ‘ö ˗a ˗nu ˗gɛn ‘dhö ˗gban ˗bhöpë ˗nu ˗bha ꞊mɔɔ ‘ö ‘yaa˗ bho mɛ ˗ta ‘kɔdhi ‘gü bha, ˗a ˗nu ˗bha.

‘Mɛ ˗nu ‘ö faan ‘yaa ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ˮiin ‘ö ʼwaa wo ˗de ꞊slɔɔ ˗dhɛ yö ˮyua ˗gɔ bha, ˗a ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ ‘waa pëbhee ˗tiaandhe ‘ö ˗a ˗dhɛ ‘dhö˗ ˗bha ˗wa ˗bhö, ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö; ˮiin pëbhee ‘yaa ꞊mɔɔ ˗a ˗nu ˗ta. ‘Mɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗bhöpë ˗saan ˗ya ˗nu ˗bha. ˗A ˗wɔn ‘gü ˮyua ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ‘mɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha ˗a ˗nu ˮdhiʋ̈ ꞊slɔɔ ˗wo ‘gbɛ. 

꞊Ya kë ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë ˗nu ‘ka, ˮyua ˗nu ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗kë ˗bhöpë ˗saan kë ˗sü ˮgblʋʋ ˮpiʋ̈, wo ꞊nɛ: 

* ꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘waa ˮgla, ‘waa ˗ba wo ˗ba ˗kɔ ˗ta. ‘Waa faan ‘sü.

* ˗Wo ˗to ˮsia˗, ˮiin ˗gleng ˗tiaandhe ‘yaa kë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha. 

* ˗A ˗nu ‘gu ˗yö ˗dɔ ˗a ˗nu ˮdhiʋ̈ ‘ö˗ ˗nu dɔɔ ˗nu (˗gbe ˗nu waa˗ ˗nu ˗gɛn ˗nu) ‘wo ˗kë ˮkangkang ˗nu ‘ka.

* ˗A ‘në ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗wo ˗kë ˮwɔɔn ˗wɔɔ ˮiin ˗a ˗nu ˮdhiʋ̈ ˗yö ˗kë ˮnuaa ˗nuaa ‘ka.

* ˗A ˗nu ˗gɛn ˗nu, ˗a ˗nu wë ˗nu waa˗ ˗nu ˗kɔ ˗nu ˗wo ˗kë ˗nu wo ˗bhlasü ‘ka. ˗A ‘bha ˗nu ꞊ya kë bhiëë ˮiin pë ‘bha ˗yö ˗wo ˗nu wo ˗a ˗nu kwi ˗bha.

* ‘Në ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˮgblü ziö ˗yö ˗gwëë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha. Mɛtii ꞊bɛdhɛ waa˗ ˮkwi ꞊bɛdhɛ ˗nu bha, ˗wa ˗nu ˗gba ‘ka, ˮkɛɛ ‘yaa ˗yan. ˗A ˮgblü ziö ‘yaa yën 

* ˗A ‘bha ˗nu ꞊ya kë, ˮyua ‘bha ˗nu ˗yaan ˗yö ˗kë ˗a ˗nu ‘gü, ‘ö ˗a ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü bha˗ ‘gü, ‘ö ˗dhiëë ˗nu ‘wo dɔ ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ˮvaandhö ˮvaandhö, ˮiin ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˮtʋdhɛ ˗nu ‘wo ˗bhla ˗nu wo ꞊sië. ˗A ‘bha ˗nu ‘ka ‘zü, ˗a ˗nu ˮbhluu ˗nu bha bhiëë ˗yö ˗ya ˗a ˗nu ˗bha.

* ‘Në ˗nu ‘ö ˗bhöpë ˗saan ‘ö ˗kë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ‘kɔdhi ‘gü ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗a mɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗gɔ ˮdhɛ ˗yö ˗kë ˮwaan ˗waan ˮiin wun ‘gbɛ ‘yaa kë ˗a ˗nu ꞊gwinng˗.

*˗A ˗nu ˮyan ‘gü ˗yö ˗kë ˮluu ˗luu. 

꞊Ya ‘go ‘në ˗nu bha˗ ˗nu ‘gü, mɛ ˮgblʋ̈gblʋ̈ ‘dhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo to, ‘ö woo ꞊de ‘pö ˗bhöpë ˗saan ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗bha bha, ‘pë ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˮdhiʋ̈ ꞊slɔɔ ˗a ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ‘gü yö ꞊nɛ:

* Mɛ ‘bha ˗nu bha, faan ‘yaa kë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha. ꞊Ya ‘go mü ˗a ˗nu sëë ꞊në ‘ö bho ‘gbɛ.

* Pë ˗bhö ˗sü ˗faan ‘yaa kë ˗a˗nu ˗gɔ.

* Bhiëë ‘yaa ˮkan ˗a ˗nu ˮdhi ˮgʋ̈ng ˮpiʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ˗nu ‘gü.

* ˗A ˗nu ˗gɛn ˗nu ˗wo ˗kë ˗bhla ˗sü ˗nu ‘ka ˮiin ‘zü ‘gbinki ˗gbinki ‘ka.

ˮYua ‘bha ˗nu ˗wo mü ˗a ˗nu ˗gɛn ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗bha ‘ö ˗gban ‘wɔn ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗bha, ˮkɛɛ ˗a ˗gbɛ ˗dhɛ ‘gü, ˗yö ˗sü pebhee yaa ˗bhö ˗sü ˗nu ˗bha.

˗A ˮyua ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, wo ˗mü:

mɛ zuëˮ ˗ta ˗ma ˗sü ˗nu, mɛ ˮtʋ ‘gü vi ˗sü ˗nu, ꞊gbaɔdhɛ ˗bha ‘në ˗nu ‘sü ˗sü ˗nu, ˗gɔ ‘gü ‘wü ˗nu, ꞊gwan ˗bha ˗kan mɛ ˗ta ˗sü ˗nu, mɛ kwi ˗bha ˮkpɛa ‘kpɔ ˗sü ˗nu, ˮyua ˗bha ˗ya mɛ ˮbhluu ˗bha ˗sü ˗nu waa˗ mɛ zuëˮ ˗kë ˗nɛɛsü ˗sü ‘ö ‘wɔn ˗nu ‘gü, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka.

˗Kwaa ‘wɔn dɔ˗ ‘ka ꞊dhɛ pebhee ˗tiaandhe ˗bhö ˗sü bha, ˗yö mɛ ˗dhü ˗takɔɔ ˮyua ˗nu ˗gɔ. ˗Bhöpë ˗së ˗nu bha, ˗wa ˗kë ‘ö mɛ kwi ‘ö dɔ ˮyua ˗gɔ ˗gɔn ˗yan ‘gü.

•  ˗Yö ˗së kö ‘kwa ˗a dɔ ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ˗bhöpë ‘ö ‘yaa ˗tiaandhe, ˗a ˗bhö ˗sü bha, ˗yö mɛ ˗gba ˮyua ‘gbɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië˗ ˗nu ‘tɔ ma- bha, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. ꞊Ya ‘go mü ˮyua ‘dhɛ ˮʋʋ ‘dhɛ ‘ö nu ‘mɛ ‘ö pebhee ˗saan ‘dhö ˗bha, ˗a mɛ ˗gɔ, ˗a ˗mɛ ‘yaa ꞊mɔɔ˗ ˗bha kö ˗yö dɔ ˗a ˮyua bha˗ ˗gɔ ˗gɔn ˗yan ‘gü. ˗A ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ kö faan ‘yaa ˗a ˗mɛ ˗bha.
• 


• ‘Në ˗nu ‘ö ‘waa pë ˗tiaandhe ˗bhö bha, kö ˮglüziö ˗yö nu ˗a ˗gɔ, ˗yö ˗kë ˮgbɩɩ˗. ˗A ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ꞊ya kë, ˗a ˗nu ˗gɔ ˗yö ˗to ˗a ‘gü.
• 
• ꞊Kpiëë kaa˗ ‘gü, ‘yaa ˗së ‘në ˗nu ‘ö pëbhee ˗saan ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗bha ‘kɔdhi ‘gü, ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ‘ka. ˗A ˗gɛn ˗mü ꞊dhɛ ˗yö ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö˗ ˗nu zë.
• 
• ‘Në ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗foodɔn ‘yaa ˮkan ˗a ˗nu kpö ‘gü. ꞊Ya ‘go mü ˗yaa pö yöö ˗a ˗nu kë, ˗ya ˗nu ˗kë ˗dedewo.
• 
‘Mɛ ˗nu ‘ö ˗bhöpë ˗saan ‘ö˗ ˗nu ˗bha bha, ˮyua ˮwɛɛwɛ dë ‘ö ˗kë ‘kpin˗ ‘ka ya, ˗yaa ˗nu kë, ˗yö ˗gwëë ˗a ˗nu ˗bha ‘ö ˗kë ˮgbɩɩ˗. 

Pëbhee ˗tiaandhe ˗bhö ˗sü bha, ˗yö ˮyuamɛ ˗ta ˗kun ‘ö ˗kë ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ ˮvaandhö.

Pëbhee ˗tiaandhe ˗yö ˮyua ˗bhɔ mɛ ‘kataa ꞊gblɛɛn, ‘ö go ‘mü ‘ö˗ ˗kë ‘ö ˮyuamɛ bha ‘ö ˗kë ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ ˮvaandhö. Yö ꞊në ˗a ˗wɔn ‘gü, ‘yö ˮyua ‘dhö ‘mɛ ‘ö˗ kë sië, ˗a ˗dhɛ ‘dhö ˗a ˗bha kö ˗a ˗mɛ ˗yö pë ˗tiaandhe ˗bhö.

˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö kwa ˗dhü ˗bhawɔn ‘dhö˗ ˗nu ˗bha kö ‘kwa˗ ˗nu ˗a ˗dhɛ 

˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö̈ kwa ˗bhawɔn ‘dhö˗ ˗nu ˗bha kö ‘kwa ˗a –nu ˗bhö kö ‘kwa ‘to kwa faan ‘gü ˗së ‘ka ˮtʋ̈ng ꞊gban ‘gü bha, ˗a ˗nu ˗gɔɔ ˗yö ˗yiisiö. ˗A ˗dhɛ ˗ya ˗bha kö ‘pë ‘ö ‘kwa dho ˗a ˗bhö yi ꞊gban ‘ka bha, ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sü ˗a ˗gɔɔ ˗yiisiö bha ˗a ˗nu ‘gü ˗dɔɔndhö ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ˗da ‘ko ˮpiʋ̈ kwaa˗ pëbhee ‘ö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ˗bha, ˗a ‘gü.

˗Bhöpë ˗gɔɔ ˗yiisiö ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha ˗a,

kpö ˗gɔɔ ˗blɛɛsü ˗mü:

1) ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo kwa ꞊nëng, kwa ˗tëng, kwa zuëˮ ga waa˗ kwa ˗dhɛ ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo kwa ‘gü ˗a ˗nu ˗gɔ yö ‘kwëë˗ ˗së ‘ka, ˗wo ˗mü. ˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha wo ꞊në ‘ö mɛ ˗yaa ˗nu ˗bhö ‘yö mɛ ˗yö ꞊kpɛa mɛ kpɛa˗ ˗kɔ ˗ta ˗së ˗dede ‘ka. ‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ ˮpiʋ̈ ‘ö kë ö kwi ‘gü, ‘ö kë ö faan ‘gü ˗a ˗dhɛ ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗dhɛkpaɔyi ꞊gban ‘ka ˗yö ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö ˗tiaandhe ‘ka ˗ya ˗zo ‘kun. ˮKɛɛ ˗yö kë ˗a ‘dhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗tun ˗së, ‘ö ‘wii see˗ kö ˗a ˗nu ‘ka.

Wo ˗mü: 

1) ˗tɔyaan, wü, ˗tɔ, ‘yuöö˗ ˮkpɛa, ˮnɔnɔ, ˮnɔnɔ ꞊kplü ‘kun ˗sü, ꞊kɛnng, ˮtʋʋ ˗dhɛ ‘gü -pë ˗nu ‘ka.

2) ˗A ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘wo dɔ ˗a ˗dhɛ ˗nu bha ˗a ˗nu ˮpiʋ̈ wo ˗mü:

ze ˮkpɛa, ˮgwɛɛ, ze suu ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ‘sozia, , kplɔɔˮ, karɔtö, 

3) ‘Yö a ‘dhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ˗nu ga doseng në ‘ö ˗bhöpë ‘ka ꞊dhɛ ˗mlü ‘ö ‘wo ˗a zɔn wöng ‘ka ˗a ‘dhö, ˮklëën ˗nu ‘dhö, ‘wo dɔ mü. 

˗Bhöpë ˮpɛpɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië ˗a ˗nu ‘tɔ ma˗ bha, ˗yö ˗së kö ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu kaan˗ ˮkwëë kwaa˗ pëbhee ‘gü. ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö. Kwa ˗mɔɔ ˗a ˗bha ‘ö ‘kwa:1, 2, 3 ˗nu bha, ˗a ˗nu ‘bha ‘në ‘bha ꞊kaan ˮkwëë kwaa˗ pëbhee ˗nu ‘gü. ˗Kwaa kë ˮdhʋ̈ yi ꞊gban ‘ka. 

˗A kpö ˗gɔɔ ꞊plɛ ˗naa: ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮsiʋ̈ ˗ya mɛ kwi ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo ‘nii˗ ˗da mɛ ‘gü

˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha, ˗wo ꞊dhɛ ˮwɔ ‘ö ˗ya ˮsiʋ̈ ˗bha, ˗a ‘dhö. ‘Mɛ ‘ö yë ˗kë ˮgbɩɩ˗ ˗dedewo, ˗a ˗bhawɔn ˗ya ˗bha kö ˗ya ˗nu ˗bhö. Wo ˗mü pë ˮnɛɛ ˗nɛɛ ˗nu waa˗ ˗a ‘dhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë ꞊dhɛ baa ˗nu ‘dhö ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. ˮKɛɛ ‘yaa ˗së kö mɛ ˗yö mɛ ˗gɔ ˗gban woo doseng ˗zë ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ˗nu ‘gü. ˗Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ faan ˗yö ˗go mɛ ˗bha. ˮSukadhu ˗pë ˗nu bha wo ˗mü: ˮsukadhu ˗dede ˗ya ˗a ‘dhö, ˮzɔyɔn ‘dhö, glɔɔ ˮnɛɛ ˗nɛɛ ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. 

꞊Ya ‘go mü, ‘pë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë ꞊dhee kë ˗pë ˗nu ‘ka woo ꞊de ‘pö kwa ˗bhawɔn ˗ya ˗nu ˗bha.

Wo në ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë ꞊dhee ˗ya ˗pë ˗nu waa˗ bhɛ ˗ya pë ˗nu ‘ka. Wo ˗mü: köng, ˗mlü, ˮklëën, ˮwɩsɩ, ˮkuu˗, baa, ˮplëë˗, ꞊piaa ˗glɔɔ, waa˗ ‘dhɛ ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo bhɔ ˮwɩsɩ ˗bha ‘ö ˮkwi ‘dhö˗ ˗dhɛ ‘pɔmö dö ‘tɛɛ˗, gën, doo, ꞊kɔnng kɔnngblë ˗nu ‘ö ˗da ˗a ‘ka ˗a ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗ bha, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. 

˗A kpö ˗gɔɔ ˗yaaga ˗naa ˗mü:

ˮYɔn ˗pë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë: wü ˮyɔn ˗nu, ˮyɔn ‘ö wo˗ ˗da ˮtʋʋ ˗bha ˗nu, ˮtukpɛ ˮyɔn ˗nu, ˮkwi ˗a ‘pë ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗da ‘bluu˗ ‘gü ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ‘bëë˗, ˗a ˗nu, ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö wo ˗kë ˮgwɛɛ ˗nu, ˮdhʋngbhɛɛ ˗nu, ze ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗dhɛ ‘sozia ˗nu, ˮkpako ˗nu , ꞊vokaa ˗nu waa˗ ˮnɔnɔ ˗nu ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. 

˗A ‘dhɛ ‘ö ‘kwa ‘go sië ˗a ˗nu ma bha, kwa kwi ˗bhawɔn ˗ya ‘sɛɛnnë ‘sɛɛnnë ˗bha. ˮKɛɛ ˗kwaa ‘gü ma ˗së ‘ka ꞊dhɛ, ˮyɔn ˗pë ˗bhö ˗sü ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗ziö ˗naa ‘gü bha ‘yaa ˗së.

˗A kpö ˗gɔɔ ˗yiisiö ˗naa ˗mü

˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˗kë kwa ˗dhü ˗takɔɔ ˗pë ˗nu ‘ka ˮyua ˗gɔ ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. Wo ꞊në ‘ö ‘wo pëbhö ˗sü ˗dhɔ ˗da mɛ ˗bha, ‘ö ‘wo faan ˗da mɛ ‘gü, ‘ö ‘wo mɛ ꞊yɔɔn ˗kë ‘gbɛ .˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo ˮdhʋ̈ bha wo ꞊në ‘ö ‘wo ˗a˗ ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘yö kwa ˗dhü ‘gü ˗dhɛ ‘ö ˗kë ˗tiaandhe, ‘ö kwa ꞊yɔɔn ‘ö ˮta sü ˗së ˗dede ‘ka kwa ‘gü. ‘Kwaa˗ ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sië ˮtʋ̈ng ‘ö ˗a ˗nu ‘gü, ˮyua ˗yö kwa ˗kë. Woo do bha ꞊në ‘ö ‘wo ꞊yɔɔn ˗da kwa ‘gü. Wo ꞊në ‘ö ‘wo˗ ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘yö kwa ga ˗nu, kwa ˮsɔn ˗nu ˗wo to ˮslʋ̈ʋ̈slʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ‘gü. 

Wo ˗mü: wü ˮbhluu ˗nu, ˗tɔyaan ˗nu, ‘yuöö˗ ˗nu, ˮnɔnɔ ˗sɛa ˮiin ꞊kplü ‘kun ˗sü ˗nu, ‘pë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo go ˮtʋʋ ˗dhɛ ‘gü ( ˮiin ziaadɛnng ‘gü) ˗nu, ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu, ˮyɔn ˮpuu ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka. ˗Bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ga ˗bhö ꞊dhɛ ˗mlü ‘dhö, ˗a ˗nu ‘ka.

Mɛ ‘gbɛdhɛ ˗wo pë ˗bhö, ˮkɛɛ ‘waa ˗a ˗bhö ꞊dhɛ ˗kɔ ‘ö˗ ˗dhɛ ‘dhö˗ ˗bha ꞊dhɛ ˗wa ˗bhö ˗a ‘ka, ˗a ‘dhö. ˗Bhöpë kpökpö ˗gɔɔ ˗yiisiö ‘ö ‘kwa ˗a ˗nu ‘tɔ ma bha, mɛ ‘bha ˗nu ˗zë ˗wo wo ˗gɔ ˗gban ˗a ˗gɔɔ doseng në˗ ˗bhö ˗sü ‘gü. ˗Mlüga ‘dhö, baa ‘dhö, ꞊piaa ˗glɔɔ waa˗ köng (ˮkpɛa) ꞊në ˗a ˗nu ˗bhö ˗sü ‘gü ‘ö ‘wo dho˗ ‘ka. ˗A ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü bha ‘yaa ˗së. ‘Ka ˗a kë ˮdhʋ̈, kö ‘kaa pë ˗bhö ˗tiaandhe ‘ka. ˗bhöpë ˗nu ‘ö ‘wo go ˗a kpö ˗gɔɔ ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ‘gü ꞊dhɛ: ˗tɔyaan ‘dhö, wü ‘dhö, ‘yuöö˗ ‘dhö, ze ‘dhö, ˮgwɛɛ ‘dhö, ˮtʋʋ ˮdhɛ ˗nu, ˮdhü bhɛ ˗nu waa˗ ˮwɛɛ ‘bha ˗nu ‘dhö, ˗kwaa ˗nu ˗bhö ‘pö ˗nu wo. ˗A ˗kë ˮdhʋ̈ ˗sü bha ꞊në pë ˗tiaandhe ˗bhö ˗sü ‘ka. ꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘yö mɛ dho ‘to˗ ˮklʋ̈ʋ̈klʋ̈ ˗dhɛ ‘gü.

30 ˮYan kë ˗yua (Apolo)

Apolo ‘ö ‘mɛ ‘ö˗ kë sië ˗a ˮdhɛ ꞊nɛ. ˗A ˗mɛ ˗yö baa ˮdhɛ ˗kpa, ˗a ˮyi bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya yö ö ˮyënng

˗Yö ˗ziö apolo ˗gɔ ꞊dhɛ mɛ ˗yö ˗më ˗kë.

31 ‘Mɛ ‘ö˗ ˗bha gɔɔn- -dhɛ ‘yaa –tiaandhe

ˮDhü ‘në ‘bha ˗yö ˗dhö, mɛ ‘gbɛ ˗dhɛ ˗wa ˗kë döng ˮdhü ‘ka. ˗Yö ˮziɔɔn ˗ziɔɔn ‘ka ꞊ni. ˮGwɛɛtaa ˗mɛ ˗nu ˗wa ˗dhɛ ꞊ziɔnng. ˗A ˮdhɛ bha, ‘mɛ ‘ö faan ‘yaa ˗a ˗bha gɔɔndhɛ ˗bha, ˗a ˗mɛ ˗ya ˮdhɛ bho kö ˗ya ˗da ˮyɔɔ ˮpiʋ̈, ˗yö ˗slëë ‘në ‘bha kë˗ ˗bha, kö ˗ya ꞊gban ˗da ‘kwëë˗ ˗ya ˗nu zɔn. ꞊Ya ö bo˗ zɔn ˗sü ‘ka, ˗ya ˗da we ˮpuu ‘në sɛɛnnë ˮpiʋ̈ ˗ya mü. ꞊Bɛdhɛ ˗së ˗dede ˗mü.

32 ˮYi -bha -go mɛ kwi ‘gü -sü

‘Në ‘gbɛ -dhɛ -wo mü ‘ö ˮgblü ziö -ya yö -a –nu -bha ‘ö - -nu -gɔ ‘ö to- ‘gü. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ ˮyi ꞊ya ‘go -a -nu kwi ‘gü. ˮYi -bha -go mɛ ‘gü -sü bha, -a ‘gbɛ -dhɛ -yö -sü ˮgblü ziö ˮgbɩgbɩ -nu në- -a -nu -bha. -Ziaanwo kö -pë -yö -da –a ‘gü, kö -a -ta -kpɛɛ ꞊ya dɔ do. ˮYi yö -mɔɔ -a -bha ‘ö go mɛ ˮgblʋ̈gblʋ̈ -nu kwa kwi ‘gü, ˮkɛɛ ‘në -nu ꞊në -a -nu -bha ‘dhö ˮgbɩɩ-. ˮYua bha, -ya -nu -zë ˮvaandhö ˮvaandhö. ꞊Ya kë ˮdhʋ̈, kö -yö -së kö ‘mɛ ‘ö ˮyi ‘ö ‘go sië -a kwi ‘gü, ‘kwa -a -kɔ dɔ. Kwa -dho -a -kɔ dɔ- ‘mü ꞊dhɛ ?

-A -kɔ dɔ -kɔ ꞊nɛ:

* a –mɛ weɩˮ ‘yaa kë ‘gbɛ ˮiin ‘yaa kë -ziaanwo, ˮiin –yö -kë dhuɛngsü.

* -a –mɛ ˮkidhʋng –yö -lɔɔ

￹- a ˮdhi –yö ˮkpɛɛ -kpɔ

* -a ˮyan -nu -wo -dho ‘gü, ‘ö -a ˮyan ˮyi ‘yaa kë.

* ꞊ya kë -dee ‘në ‘ka, ꞊gwinngdhö -ya -kë.

* -a -mɛ zuëˮ -ta -yö -ma ˮvaandhö ˮvaandhö.

* -a -gɛn waa- -kɔ -nu -wo -kë -sɛa.

* -kwaa -mɛ ‘gu -ta kwi ˮgan ꞊ni: ꞊Ya kë ꞊dhɛ ‘yaa ‘dho sië ö ˮgblʋʋ ‘gü ˮvaandhö -së ‘ka, kö ˮyi ‘yaa ‘në bha- ‘gü.

‘Mɛ ‘ö ˮyi ‘ö ‘go sië- ‘gü, -a ꞊bɛdhɛ ꞊nɛ:

-A -mɛ -yö ˮyi mü ‘gbɛ. -Yö ˮdhü bhɛ -nu ˮyi mü. -Yö ˮtʋʋ ˮyi ˮlʋ̈nglʋ̈ng -nu pa. 

‘Pë ‘ö ya -kaa kë kö ‘ka- nu -a -dhɛ: -ka ˮyi -sanngdhe (-zuɛɛbhɛ) ˮiin ‘zü ‘dhiitrë do kë ˮwɔsü. ꞊Ya ꞊dhiëë kö ‘ka ˮsang ˮgblʋ̈gblʋ̈ bha, -a-yan ꞊plɛ dan ˮsukadhu -bi ˮiin ˮzɔyɔn, ˮiin ‘zü ˮsukadhu kpö ˮsɔɔdo ˮiin ‘zü ‘bhawo ˮsang ‘sɛɛnnë bha, -a -yan ˮsɔɔdo dan ˮsukadhu ‘ka. ‘Ka ‘go mü kö ‘ka ˮsang sɛɛnnë bha, -a -yan do ‘ö- -ta ‘ö ˮkan -sü ‘ka ꞊wee bi ˮpiëën -piëën ‘ka -a ‘dhö, ‘seng- ˮyi ˮSang ‘në ‘sɛɛnnë -yan do ‘dhö ( ˮni kö ˮyua -mɛ bha ‘yaa -pe sië). Pë ˮpɛpɛ bha -kaa -nu kaan- ˮkwëë. ꞊Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ˮiin -deenë ‘ka, kaa nu- -dhɛ ˮsang ‘ka. -Kaa nu- -dhɛ -dedewo ꞊sɔbhɛɛ ‘ka. ꞊Ya kë ꞊dhɛ ‘në bha -a ˮgblü ‘dhö ziö sië, kë ˮdhʋ̈ ‘ö ‘ka ˮyi nu -a -dhɛ ‘ö- mü. -Kaa- -bha ˮyi kë ˮbhaa ˮyi ˮö ‘wo- kun ˮbhaa -ta –a ‘ka.

-Kaa nu -a -dhɛ ‘yënng- -kɔ dan ˮsɔɔdhu ˮsɔɔdhu ‘ka (minitë ˮsɔɔdhu ˮsɔɔdhu ‘ka), -yö ‘to-‘ka ˮdhʋ̈ -yö -ya ö weɩˮ bho –sü -bha -së ‘ka.

꞊Ya kë mɛ ‘kpii- ‘ka, -yaa pö yöö ˮyi mü, -yö ˮyi ‘dhiitrë ꞊plɛ ˮiin ö -ziö -ta -a mü -dhɛkpaɔyi -bha. 

꞊Ya kë ‘në sɛɛnnë ‘ka, ‘yii -a mü ‘gbɛ, -yö kë ˮyi ‘dhiitrë do -dhɛkpaɔyi -bha.

꞊Ya kë ꞊tɔn ꞊dhɛ ‘wɔn ˮpɛpɛ bha ‘ka -nu kë kö ‘yaan -yan sië, -ka ‘dho ꞊dhɔtrɔɔ ꞊plöö.

33 ˮGblü ziö

Ka ˮgblü ‘dhö ziö sië:

• -ka -bhöpë ‘ö ˮKwi ‘dhö- -dhɛ karɔtë bha, -a -kpa ˮwɛɛwɛ -së ‘ka. ꞊Ya ma, -a ˮyi ‘dhö oo, -a karɔtë bha ‘dhö oo, -ka ꞊wee ‘në ‘bha kë- -bha kö ‘ka -a ˮyi bha mü, ‘ka- karɔtë -bhö.
• 
• -Ka gwɛ bhɛ ‘ö go ö -dhü ‘gü -dee ‘gü bha, -a ‘sü. -Kaa ˮkɛɛ bho- -	bha, kö ‘ka- -da ˮyi ‘ö ˮsukadhu ‘dhö- -bha, -a ꞊bhaa. ꞊Ya ‘ma- -bha ꞊së ‘ka, kö ‘ka- mü.
• 
• -Ka glɔɔ -pëkë -sü (tan -sü) -bhö.

34 ˮZɔn ˮyɔn bha ꞊bɛdhɛ -mü

Miëë -ya kë ü -bha, ‘ö ‘yaa ga sië, ˮZɔn ˮyɔn –ya –a ‘gü.

1. ʼWaa ʼwɔn yaa "yɔɔbho ʼwɔn yaa ʼka

-Kwɛ -zlaan ʼö ya, -kwɛ -zlaan zii -dede –mü.

"Tϋng ʼbha ʼgü Gbaa" ꞊plöö, ʼyö gɔndë ʼnë do ʼbha bha -a -bha dhebë ʼö ʼnë gɔɔn- do kpɔ. ʼNë ʼö "dhϋ bha, -sëdhɛ ʼö gun- -gɔ -a "suma "yɔɔ ʼyaa gun "tϋng ʼkö bha- ʼgü tongtongdhö.

-A -ga ꞊dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka, ʼyö waa- ö dhe ʼwo dho "dhɔɔ ʼgü "kwi -pö ʼgü Gbiaan ꞊gwinng- . ꞊Dhɛ ʼö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö ö bo "dhɔɔ dɔ -sü ʼka, ʼyö pö yöö ö yeekë kö ʼö ʼdho ö -yɛɛbhaa ʼpödhö, ʼyö gɔ sü. Gɔ ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya kwa -mɔɔ -a -bha ʼö ʼkwa- -dhɛ -yakwëë -kë ʼgü -gɔ. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ -wa -ya ʼgü, mɛ ꞊gban -wo wo wë -bɔ ʼkwëë-. "Kwi -nu -wo woo- pë -dhɛ basie. -A "tϋng ʼö bha- ʼgü, kö ziaan -yö -tun ʼya- -dedewo. Ziaan bha -a -tadhɛ ʼbha -yö -gun mü, ʼyaa gun -së tongtongdhö. "Yi ga ʼkpii- nü ʼö gun -tɔn ꞊plɛ ꞊zinng ʼgü. -Wa -tɔn ꞊lɔɔ "wɛ ꞊ni, ʼyö ʼwo loo pɔng -ta. Pɔng bha- "kan -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö -wa ʼto ꞊wa -ya -tɔn ʼkun -sü -bha. Pɔng ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya, ʼwaa ꞊mɔɔ- -bha kö -wa -zɔn kwaa- pɔng -nu ʼö ʼwo ꞊dɛɛ ʼpö- -nu ʼgü ya, -a -nu -bha -sëdhɛ ʼka. ʼNë ʼö bha -a -bha -sëdhɛ -wɔn ʼgü, ʼdho ʼö ʼwo gun- wo sië gɔ ʼgü bha, mɛ ʼbha -yaa ʼsü, -yaa -ga, ʼyö mɛ ʼbha ʼdhö- sü. -A -bha -sëdhɛ -zë -a -zɔn ʼka "wɛɛ ʼbha ʼyii kë ꞊slɔɔ ʼnu do, "iin ʼyii ʼdho ꞊slɔɔ- "kpʋng ꞊taa ʼö to- ʼka "dhϋ ʼö -kë "dhiëng "dhiϋ ʼto -dhɛ -zë -a ʼka. -A -nu -loo pɔng -ta "tϋng -dede bha kö ʼnë bha -yö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë do ʼbha -gɔ. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë ꞊dhɛ gɔ -yö -gun zuu" -zuu zuu" kë sië yaa ʼka bha, ʼyö ʼmɛ ʼö bha ʼö ʼnë bha- ꞊nëng ö -tong -bha. Kwa- ʼwɔn -dɔ ꞊dhɛ gɔ -yaa pö yöö -tɔn ʼkun, ʼyö -a "dhiϋ "ta ʼsü -mɛ -yaa kë, ʼyö -ya -ya ʼka -tɔn -bha -bɛng ʼka, kë "dhϋ kö gɔ ʼya ʼdho pö ʼö bhɔ ö zü ʼka. ꞊Ya -tɔn ʼkun, ʼyö gun -naa ʼgbaannu.

-A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- ʼgü, -a vuu" -mü -vuu -mü vuu" -mü ʼö gun kë sië bha, kö gɔ -yö ꞊zang "zang kë sië.

"Eke kwa dë -nu -wa -pö : « Piaa" -yaa -mɛ ʼyaa- pö kwa ziaan -ta ꞊plɛ. » -kaa -ga, ʼyö ʼnë bha ʼö bɔ ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha- gban -ta, ʼyö bɔ gɔ ʼö bha- yɛ ʼka, ʼyö -pö "yi ꞊bhaa ; ʼyö mɛ ꞊gban ʼwo -ya "gbla -sü -bha "gbʋ ʼka ꞊dhɛ : « N dhee" -nu -gblü bhoo, ʼya ga bhoo, -ka "ta yi -dhɛ bhoo. -Zlaan ü ꞊wɛ ꞊ee ? »

Gɔ ꞊sofɛɛ ꞊de ʼpö -a -bha ʼgü, gɔ ꞊zuu "zuu ʼö kë sië bha nü- -wɔn ʼgü ʼyö mɛ -nu bha ʼwo "wɩ sië bha. ʼYaa- ʼwɔn dɔ ꞊dhɛ ʼnë ʼbha -ya -pö "yi ꞊bhaa. ʼKö ʼzü yöö- ʼwɔn dɔ ꞊zɔɔ ꞊wɛ, -a -dhɛ -ya -bha kö -yö -tɔn ʼkun ꞊kö -blɛɛsü kö -yö gun -naa gɔ ʼgbaannu ; ʼyii kë kë "dhϋ gɔ -yö -dho bhɔ ö zü ʼka, ʼö nu ʼö -pö "yi ꞊bhaa. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ ʼyö -tɔn kun ʼyö ʼdɔɔnnu. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë ꞊dhɛ dhebë ʼnë bha -yö -gun -a "piϋ ꞊dhɛ ʼö ʼdho ʼköö -pö ö bha ʼnë bha- ꞊keng- "yi ꞊bhaa bha, ʼyö ʼwo- kun kö ʼya dho ö -de zë-. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ gun ʼö- wo "dhϋ bha, kö "yi bha ꞊ya pa, kö ꞊ya wɔ "wɛ mɔngdhö -ziisü ʼka ꞊ni. -A ʼklɔɔ- -mü ꞊dhɛ -yö -gun "dhϋ dha ban "tϋng ʼgü. ꞊Ya ʼgo mü -a gɔɔn- "piϋ, dhe "piϋ, ʼmɛ ʼö yöö kë "yi kë -mɛ -tiaandhe ʼka -a -nu ꞊zinng ʼgü mü, ʼyaa gun.

"Siasia bha, ʼyö ʼwo dho ꞊zang -nu -dhɛ Gbiaan ꞊gwinng-. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo nu ʼyö ʼwo dhɛa" ʼkpɔ -kë -dhɛ -dede ʼö ʼnë bha ʼö -pö -a -bha bha -a -wɔn ʼka. ʼYö ʼwo glɔɔ -dhü do -kan, ʼyö ʼwo- -zuö -dhɛ -dede ʼö ʼnë bha ʼö kë -pö -a -bha bha- ʼgü, ʼyö glɔɔ ꞊gbë bha ʼö dho ʼö -wo -dhɛ ʼbha ʼgü "yi -gɔ "siaa- ꞊yën mü. ʼWo dho ʼdho- wo bhɔɔ" bho mü, kö ʼnë bha -a ꞊gee nü ꞊wɛɛ, -ya ga. ʼWɔn bha -yö -gun ꞊dhɛ -gblü ʼdhö, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-, -yö -gun -wëësü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ ʼyö ꞊zang -nu ʼwo "klɩɩ -ya dhebë ʼnë bha- -kɔɔ kö ʼya ʼdho ö -de zë-. ʼYö ʼwo ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha, -a -bha -kë ʼpö "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwo dho -a -nu ʼka ꞊zang ꞊plöo Gbiaan ꞊gwinng-, ʼyö ʼwo dhebë ʼnë bha- -da ʼkɔ do ʼbha ʼgü, ʼyö ʼwo ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha, -a -bha -kë ʼpö "dhϋ. ʼYö ꞊zang -nu bha ʼwo -ziö ʼwo dho Gbaa" ꞊plöö. ʼWo ꞊loo mü ʼyö dhebë ʼnë bha -a ꞊gɔn ʼö -dhɛ ʼö -bha ʼyö ʼwo- -dhɛ -zɔn -a -nu -dhɛ kö waa- ö "tɛɛbë -nu -wo "maa gɔɔn- sië. ꞊Dhɛ ʼkö ʼwo -kpan -a -bha -zë bho bhoo, "klɩɩ- nü ʼö ʼwo- -ya -a -kɔɔ, ʼwo nu- ʼka Gbiaan ꞊gwinng-. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo ꞊loo mü, ʼyö ʼwo dhebë ʼnë waa- nëglɔɔnʼ ʼnë bha -a -nu yö "kpɛnng. ꞊Dhɛ ʼkö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö -kpan ö ꞊gɔn -bha, "pɛ ʼö- bho "gbʋ -bha, -a -wo -yö -kë ꞊dhɛ dha "wɩ -wo ʼdhö.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwo -ziö ʼwɔn bha- ʼgü -a ꞊gɔn -dhɛ. ʼYö gɔndë ʼnë bha ʼö ʼdɔɔnnu zuudhö ꞊dhɛ ʼmɛ ʼö -kling kling- ꞊ya yö nü wo- -ta ʼdhö. ʼYö go ʼmü ʼö- pö ꞊zang -nu -dhɛ -wo "klɩɩ bho ö -kɔɔ. ʼYö ʼwo- bho mü. ʼYö dho ʼö ꞊yɔɔn nëglɔɔnʼ ʼnë bha- "sɔɔ, ʼyö ö "yan -gban -a ʼgü zuudhö. ʼÖ gun kë sië "dhϋ bha, kö ꞊zang -nu -wa ꞊yɔɔn- -nu "sɔɔ mü. ʼYö gɔndë ʼnë bha ʼö- pö piaa" yaa- -mɛ bha- -dhɛ : « N "tɔngdë, ʼwɔn ʼö ü "dhiϋ ꞊slɔɔ bha ʼyii kë kë ü ꞊kwɛng- -wɔn ʼka. ʼBhii kë- "dhiϋ wlüü" -a -bha. -Zlaan këwɔn -mü. N ʼdhu do -yö ʼpödhö, ʼma- nu ü -dhɛ dhe ʼka. Kö -yö kë ꞊dhɛ ʼwɔn ʼö -kë bha -ya dhi nü ʼö- wo n -dhɛ, ʼyaa -mü, "kɛɛ ʼwɔn -yake nü ʼö ʼa- -ya... ».

-Dedewo, ʼyö gɔndë ʼnë bha ʼö- pö -kɔ ʼö- -bha, ʼö- -kë -a -kɔta, ʼyö ʼmɛ bha waa- ʼdhu ʼwo to wo ʼko -gɔ. ʼNë -nu ʼö ʼwo- -nu kpɔ, ʼmɛ ʼö- -gɔ ʼgü ʼyii kë kë -së, ʼö ʼyii kë ʼdho ꞊klang ʼka ꞊gblɛɛn, yö nü ʼö kë -kë ꞊klang- -gɔ -mɛ ʼka, "kɛɛ ꞊klang- -gɔ -mɛ -nu -bha didhɛtëë ʼka. Mɛ "pɛpɛ ʼdhɛ ʼkö ʼwo to, -a -nu ꞊gban -wo kë -kë "kwi -gɔ -mɛ "gblϋgblϋ -nu ʼka.

Gɔndë ʼnë ʼö bha -ya -zɔn kwa -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ -de -kun ʼwɔn "dhiϋ -sü, nü ʼö -së. ʼWɔn -yake -ya -sü, ʼö ʼbhaa ʼwɔn yaa "yɔɔ bho ʼwɔn ʼyaa ʼka, nü ʼö -së.

2. -Dhioo -wo ʼyaa ziaan yaa -zɔn mɛ -dhɛ

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka ʼyö laabhölaa ʼö -kë wü -naa -gblüdë ʼka, ʼö wü ꞊gban "pɛpɛ -dhɛ ö -kuu "dhiϋ : ꞊soo- -ta -wü -nu oo-, -ta ʼgu -ta -wü -nu oo-, -maa -nu oo, a n ʼbha wü "pɛpɛ ʼkö ʼwo -kë -zë bho wü ʼka -a -nu ꞊gban -wo kë -nu ꞊dhiɔɔ -wo -bha. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ ʼyö laabhölaa ʼdhö dhiang sü ʼyö- pö : « Ma "sɛ ʼgü -mɛ -nu, -dhɛ ꞊ya ꞊kpaɔ ka -bha -ee ? Ka nuwɛɛ "sɛ -bha mü ? Ka nuwɛɛ ka -de gaa- yë -bha mü ? Kö ʼka ꞊gwëë, ʼka -ya n -dhɛ "gbɩɩ- bha ʼaa -yö kë ? Kö ka dhɔɔbhaa -wɔn ʼö ʼdhö -Zlaan Atanna ʼö yö nü mɛ ꞊gban kwa -zo yö- -dhɛ ʼka, kö -ya kë ka -dhɛ ʼdɔɔndhö bha ʼaa -yö kë ? Kö kaa- ʼnë -nu -wo -ya ka -dhɛ pinngdhö, kö ʼmɛ ʼdhɛ -nu ʼö dhe ʼyaa- -nu -gɔ, kö -wo dhe -së ʼsü, kö -wa ʼgü ʼnë -së ʼkpɔ, kö ꞊sii -yö kë -a -nu ʼgü bha ʼaa -yö kë ?

Kö kaa- ʼnë ʼdhɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo "kwi ꞊plöö, ʼö "kwi ꞊plöö -dhɛ -bha -kë -a -nu -bha "gbɩɩ- -sü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼpë ʼö kwa dë -nu ʼwaa- -bhö ʼö ʼwo dho ʼwo- -bhö, dhe ʼö kwa dë -nu ʼwaa zun- -bha, ʼö ʼwo dho ʼwo zun- -bha, -dhɛ ʼö kwa dë -nu ʼwaa- -ga, ʼö ʼwo dho ʼwo- -ga... kö biaan ʼö "dhϋ, kö -yö ʼgo -a -nu -bha bha ʼaa -yö ʼgo -oo ?

Nu ʼö ʼka- wo ma ꞊dhiɔɔ -wo -bha bha, ʼka -a kë -së -dedewo. Ka -dhɛ ʼö ʼa- wo bha, a- -wo "dhϋ kö ʼka ʼdho ma dhebë ʼsü -dhɛ ʼgü, ö dë -nu "piϋ. ʼMa- -yɔ kë ʼnu ʼma n bo. -A ʼsü -wɔn nü ʼö -ya ʼto. ʼMɛ -nu ʼö- -dhɛ ʼdhö- -bha ꞊dhɛ -wo -dho ʼto- n "piϋ yö kö yɛng- -nu ʼyi yi "yan ʼto ʼdho -mɛ -nu -gɔ, wo -mü : ʼpö- dë -nu, ʼpö- dhe -nu, -kwɛɛ ʼnë -nu, "nɛɛ- ʼnë -nu waa- ʼnë ʼsɛɛnnë -nu ʼka. ꞊Ya ʼgo yö -zë -a ʼgü, mɛ "pɛpɛ ʼö ʼka to, ka -dho ʼdho-. N "tɔngdhe bha -a ʼtɔ -mü ꞊Geetiinë ʼka. A- -pö ꞊Geetiinë. ʼDho ʼö kaa- wo bha, kö ʼka ʼtɔ "wɛɛ pö, ka -bha ʼö kaa- -slɔɔ ʼgü, kö ka -ta -wɔn -mü. Kö ʼka ma, ʼka ꞊gwëë n -dhɛ bha ʼaa -yö kë ? -Ka ʼdho.

-A -pö mü ꞊dhɛ ka -dho ꞊loo mü ꞊dɛɛ. -A -nu "yan -yö ka -gɔ ꞊dhɛ "gwannë -yö ö "yan -to -mɔɔ -gɔ. ʼKa ʼtɔ "wɛɛ pö -wo -dho ka -ma. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ -wo -dho ka ʼsü ꞊dhɛ ꞊kwan -mɛ -nu ʼdhö. Kö ʼka ʼdho, kö kaa- "ta -yö dhi bha ʼaa -yö kë -oo ? » ʼYö ʼwo- pö : « -A ʼmii -na »

"Aa, ʼyö wü -nu bha ʼwo -da ziaan- "tan bho -sü ʼka ʼö ʼwo- pö : « -Ɛɛ ꞊Geetiinë wee, ꞊Geetiinë.-Ɛɛ ꞊Geetiinë wee, ꞊Geetiinë. -Ɛɛ ꞊Geetiinë wee, ꞊Geetiinë. -Ɛɛ ꞊Geetiinë wee, ꞊Geetiinë. » A n ʼbha yuudhö -së ʼka ꞊ni ʼö wo dho- ʼka. -A -ga, ziaan -bha -kë ꞊gblɛɛn -sü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼö dɔ mü kö din- -yaa -nu ʼkun. ʼWo dho ʼwo ꞊loo -dhɛ ʼbha bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ʼwo -kan sö -blaa do ʼbha ʼgü, kö sö ꞊gbaan -pëkë yuudhö -dhɛ "pɛpɛ ꞊gban ʼgü mü. -Kpan -a -bha -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö -wa ꞊wɛng- ʼgü, -wa -ya -a ga -bhö -sü -bha. ʼYö ʼwo- -bhö, ʼwo- -bhö, ʼwo- -bhö, ʼwo- -bhöö. -A -ga, -a -nu ꞊gban -zo ꞊ya bhɔ -gblüdë "tɔngdhe ʼtɔ ꞊Geetiinë ʼka. -Kɔ ʼö ʼmɛ ʼdhϋ yöö pë -bhö -a -bha, kö -yö ziö- ʼka ö "tɛɛdo -ta, kö yö nü -a -nu "tϋng ʼdhö- ʼgü. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -waa -bhö ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö, ʼö- -nu ʼgu ꞊ya dɔ, -ya -ya ʼka -a -nu "sɛnng-, ʼyö ʼwo ꞊wlüü kö ʼwo -da ziaan-. -A pö ʼö woo- bho ꞊geetinɔ bha, -a -nu -zo ꞊ya bhɔ -waa pö ꞊Geesöga. -Wa -ya yö nü- bho -sü -bha ꞊dhɛ : « -Ɛɛ ꞊Geesöga wee, ꞊Geesöga. -Ɛɛ ꞊Geesöga wee, ꞊Geesöga. -Ɛɛ ꞊Geesöga wee, ꞊Geesöga. » -Gɛn -së -mɛ -nu ʼkö- -nu suu ʼdhö -kë ꞊dhɛ ꞊kɔngsodhö ( ʼö yö nü ʼö wü -nu ʼö ʼwo "bü, ʼö- -nu -gɛn ʼdhö -së -a -naa -gblüdë ʼka bha-) ʼdhö bha, kö ʼpë ʼö ʼwo- kë sië wo -de ʼka, -Zlaan yöö dosɛng nü ö bha pë dɔ. ʼYö ʼtɔ bha ʼö to -a -nu "dhi ʼyö wo dho ʼwo ꞊loo- ʼka ʼpö- bha- ʼgü. -A -nu -loo mü -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ-, kö ʼpö- -mɛ -nu : ʼnë "piϋ, dhe "piϋ, gɔɔn- "piϋ, -a -nu ꞊gbaan "dhɛɛdhɛ pa -a -nu -wo -bha. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö -dhɛng -nu bha -a -nu -wo "dhiϋ ꞊loo -mɛ -yö dhiang sü ʼyö- pö : « N dë -nu, n dhe -nu ʼö ʼka ʼpö- ya- ʼgü ya, -dhɛ -ya ꞊kpaɔ. Ka nuwɛɛ yö, ka ꞊sɛɛ- yö. Ka nuwɛɛ yi ꞊gban ʼka, ʼka- -sëdhɛ yö. Kö -Zlaan -yö ka gba ꞊sii gɔɔ ꞊gblɛɛn ʼka bha ʼaa -yö kë -oo ? » ʼYö ʼpö- -mɛ -nu ꞊gban ʼwo- pö : « -A ʼmiina » ʼYö dhiang "dhiϋ ꞊loo -mɛ bha ʼö pö : « Nu ʼö ʼyi- wo- bha, yi -nu -a -së ʼgü. Yii- -gblüdë, yii- "sɛ ꞊kɔɔnmɛ, nü yi bɔ ka "piϋ ö bha dhebë ʼö -kë ka ʼdhu ʼka, -a ʼsü -dhɛ ʼgü, ꞊dhɛ -kɔ ʼö- ʼwɔn ʼö ka "yaan ʼka bha- ʼdhö. Yii- -gblüdë -ya -pö ʼka dɔ "gbɩɩ- kö yi ꞊loo -sü waa- yi yeekë -sü ꞊gban -yö ʼto ʼkwëë-. N dë -nu kö ʼka -ya yi -dhɛ "gbɩɩ- bha ʼaa -yö kë ? Kö ʼka- ʼgü ma yi -gɔ -së ʼka -Zlaan "saa- ʼgü bha, ʼaa -yö kë -maa ? ʼWɔn ʼö ʼyi nu- ʼgü, ʼyö nü ʼö -dengdeng ʼka bha. »

꞊Dhɛ ʼö ö bo- -pö "dhϋ -sü ʼka, ʼyö ꞊dhuutii ʼö ʼpö- bha- -gü bha ʼö- pö : « -Dhɛng -nu kaa- "dhɛɛdhɛ ꞊nɛ. -kaa ꞊biöö ka dhɔɔbhaa ʼka. "Tan ʼö ʼka -da ʼka ʼpödhö ya -a din -yö -së "gbɩɩ-. -Kaa ziö ʼbha bho ʼmü ꞊sië yi -dhɛ kö ʼyi ʼdho yi ʼdhu bha- baa- -dhɛ ʼgü. » -A -pö "dhϋ -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ-, kö -wo -së -mɛ -nu -wa ꞊Geesöga bha- ꞊nëng -a -bha -dedewo ꞊ya ziö- ʼka -a -blɛɛsü -ta. Yaa" ʼpö- -mɛ -nu bha -wa -kë "dhϋ kö ʼwo dɔ wo dɔ -kɔ ʼka, -a -nu -ma -yan ʼgü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ꞊dhuutii waa- ö -dɔ -bha -nu ʼwo nu, ʼyö ʼwo "tan -kan, ʼyö ʼpö- dë bha ʼö -dhɛng -nu dhɛa" kpɔ ʼö- pö : « Ma -dhɛng -nu, ʼwɔn do ʼbha nü ʼö ka -zo -yö kë bhɔ- ʼka ʼyɛɛn- ya- gü. Yö -mü kaa- -gbüdë -bha dhebë bha- ʼtɔ ʼka. -Wa -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ ?

-A -pö ꞊Geesöga -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ-, kö -wa ꞊loo- -nu -ta ꞊dhɛ -maa -yö ꞊loo -mlü -ta, -wa -ya -a -nu -ma -sü -bha. Wü ʼdhɛ -nu ʼkö -a -nu -gɛn ʼyaa "gbɩɩ- ꞊dhɛ bhaɔ -nu, "guudë -nu... ʼdhö, ʼyii kë kë -a -nu -wëë -bha ʼpödë ʼbha -nu ʼö ʼwo gun mü -a -nu kë -sü -zë -a ʼka, -a -nu -gɔ -yö -gun yöö ʼto ʼwɔn bha- ʼgü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo dho ʼwo ꞊loo wo -kɔ ʼgü "fiëë ʼka -a -naa -gblüdë -ta, ʼyö -gblüdë ʼö -ya -nu "yan ʼgü -dedewo. ʼYö- -nu dhɛa" kpɔ ꞊dhɛ ʼtɔ -mɛɛ ʼö ʼwo kë- pö ʼmü ? ʼYö ʼwo- pö ꞊Geesöga. ʼYö "fɔngfɔng -yö -da -gblüdë ʼgü, -a -nu -zo ʼö bhɔ ʼö- wo ʼtɔ bha- ʼka bha- -wɔn ʼgü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ ʼyö -maa ʼnë ʼö ʼwo- zöng -kë ʼö ö kɔngga "dhiϋ ꞊wlüü, ʼyö pö : « -Gblüdë, ʼdho ʼö ʼyi -a wo bha, ma -zë n -zo ʼyii kë bhɔ, "kɛɛ "suϋ nü ʼö ʼa kë- wo ma mɛ "gbϋgblϋ -nu -gɔ ziaan-. -A -gɛn -mü ꞊dhɛ, a -pö ʼnu -a -nu -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ ʼbhaa kë- pö ꞊Geesöga, -wo -mɔɔ -a -bha ʼnu ʼö ʼwo pö ʼma n -de ʼsü ʼwɔn dɔ -mɛ ʼka ʼma ziö ʼka- -nu -ta. ʼÖ- -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- ʼgü ʼwo n -ma. Yaa n dheebhang -nu yi -mɔɔ -a -bha ʼö ʼyi dho "vaandhö, ʼyi nu ü bha dhebë bha- ʼka. »

ʼYö -gblüdë -ya pö- -dhɛ waa- ö dheebhang -nu -wo ʼdho- ʼsü-. ʼYö zöng -nu bha ʼwo -da ziaan-. ʼYö ʼwo -ya ꞊Geetiinë -tan bha- bho -sü -bha, ʼyö ʼwo dho- ʼka "dhϋ, ʼwo ꞊loo- ʼka dhɛng- -dhɛ ʼbha bha- ʼgü, kö -a -mlü ꞊gbaan ʼto "dhϋ ꞊ya ʼwü mɔngdhö. Woo- kë -kɔ ʼö- -bha kö ʼtɔ ʼö bha ʼya ʼdho ꞊dhɛng -a -nu -gɔ bha, ʼyö ʼwo wo -pɛ ʼgü ꞊plɛ ; ʼyö -a kpö do ʼbha ʼdhö to "dhü ʼgü, ʼö -ya "tan bha- bho -sü -bha, ʼyö- kpö do ʼö ꞊lɔɔ -mlü ʼgü.

-A ʼdhɛ ʼö ʼwo gun -mlü ʼgü bha, ꞊dhɛ ʼö ʼwo pë -bhö ʼö -nu ʼgu ʼdhö dɔ ; ʼyö ʼwo dho "dhü ʼgü ʼwo "tan sü, ʼyö- ʼdhɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo gun "dhü ʼgü bha, wo -zë ʼwo ꞊lɔɔ kö ʼwo pë -bhö ʼpö.

ʼPë ʼö -kë ʼö zöng -maa kë -sü ʼö -kë "gbɩɩ- -mlü ʼwü "tϋng ʼgü bha, ʼyö bha. -Wo pë -see mɛ -bha, ꞊ya ʼgo mü -a -nu -maakëdhɛ -yö "gbɩɩ-. ꞊Ya kë –maa kë -mɛ ʼgü ꞊dhɛ -a -nu ꞊gban nü "dhü ʼgü bha, yaa" kö -a kpö ʼbha -yö -mlü ʼgü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö- -nu ꞊gban ʼwo wo bo pë -bhö -sü ʼka ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö, ʼyö ʼwo dho "tan bha- ʼka ʼwo ꞊loo- ʼka ʼpö- bha- ʼgü. -A pö -sü nü ʼö ꞊Geetiinë, kö dhebë bha -waa nu- -nu -dhɛ, ꞊wa nu- ʼka -gblüdë Laabhölaa -dhɛ. ʼWɔn bha- "dhia -ma -gblüdë ʼgü -sü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼyö ꞊gbauu ga ʼö -kë ꞊ni -a -da zöng -bha wü "pɛpɛ ꞊gban wëëdhö, -a -zo bhɔ ʼö ʼyii kë wo ʼtɔ ʼö bha ʼka ʼö- wo ʼyi bha- ʼka bha, -a -wɔn ʼgü. "Tϋng bha- ʼgü, kö ꞊gbauu bha, - a "dhiϋ -zian -yö "puu, kö- ꞊taama -dhɛ -yö -tii. Kweɩ" ʼdhu sɔ -mü ʼö ʼpödö -nu ʼwo- -da "wlaan- yi -nu ʼwo -kë : dhe ʼsü -sü -nu, ʼgbaannë troo -nu nu... ʼka, -a -nu -ta. Sɔ suu ʼö "dhϋ bha -yö -tun ꞊kö ꞊dɛɛ ꞊Yaoba -nu kwaa- "sɛ ʼgü. A suu -yö ʼgbɛ. ʼWɔndɔmɛ -nu nü ʼö ʼwo gun -a -da sië ꞊dhɛ -kɔ ʼö ʼkwa- yö sië- ʼka zöng -gɔ ya- ʼdhö.

ʼPë ʼö -kë ʼö zöng ʼgblëë- -zian ʼö -kë "puu, ʼö- ꞊taama -dhɛ ʼö -kë tii bha, ʼyö bha.

-Kwaa kë -së kö -dhioo ʼö -Zlaan, ʼö kwa dë -nu, kwa dhe -nu, kwa "tɔngdë -nu waa- kwaa- mɛ "gblϋgblϋ -nu, ʼwo dɔ -naa kwa -ta bha, kwa -zo ʼya dho bhɔ- ʼka. Kwa zuë" ʼya ʼdho pö ʼö bhɔ pë "wɛɛwɛ ʼbha -bha, ʼö ʼkwa- zë -a -wɔn -dhɛ, ʼkwa -a -naa -dhioo -wo -nu bho kwa "tʋʋ, ʼö ʼkwa -kë ʼwɔn yaa kë -mɛ -nu ʼka.

3. Dhebë ʼnë do ʼbha ʼö ö bha ʼnë dha ʼö-wo "siϋ gɔn -ziisü -gɔ -Mɔɔsii ˮsɛ ʼgü

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka -Mɔɔsii "sɛ ʼgü, ʼpödhɛ do ʼbha ʼö ʼwo- -dhɛ Bangfoodha -a ʼgü, ʼyö -Mɔɔsii dhebë do ʼbha bha, ʼö -suö dhia" "piϋ ʼö dho "yi ꞊bhaa. -Yö -to "yi ꞊bhaa mü ʼyö "siϋ ʼdhö -da -a -bha ʼkɔ dhee" ʼka -a ziaan ʼgü. Kö "siϋ ʼö ya -yö kë -go ʼmɛ, ʼyii ʼgo ʼmɛ -ee ? Mɛ ʼbha ʼyii kë ʼwɔn ꞊slɔɔ- ʼgü. ʼWo dho "kan wo -ta dosɛng, kö ʼkɔ dhee" bha -yö "gϋ sië, kö "siϋ ꞊ya ʼma- -bha "wɛ mɔngdhö -dhɛ ꞊gban ʼgü, "kɛɛ kö dhebë ʼnë bha, -a -bha ʼnë ʼnë ʼö- to yi ʼgü ʼö dho "yi ꞊bhaa, -yö ʼkɔ bha- ʼgü. -Yö "gbʋ bɔ sië ʼö ö dhe -dhɛ ʼka. ʼNë bha -a dë waa- gɔɔn- ʼgbɛ -wo -gun "kpɛnngdhö mü, "kɛɛ mɛ ʼbha -kɔ ʼyii kë ꞊mɔɔ -da ʼkɔ bha- ʼgü -sü -bha, "siϋ nɛɛ- ʼö gun ʼkɔ -bha -a "dhi -bha bha -a -wɔn ʼgü. "Yi ʼnë -nu ʼkö ʼwo gun ʼkɔ "wɛɛ -nu ʼgü, -wo kë- -nu ꞊gban -wɛnng "siϋ bha- -bha, "kɛɛ ʼyii ʼwɔn ʼbha -yan. "Yi ꞊bhaa -dhɛ ꞊de ʼpö -a -bha -kë ꞊gblɛɛn -sü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, mɛ ʼbha faan ʼyii kë dɔ -dho "yi ʼsü- -dhɛ ʼgü. Woo- kë ꞊dhɛ ? ꞊Klingkling ꞊ya yö- -nu -ta. -Yö -to yö nü- ʼgü, ʼyö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö nu.

-A ꞊loo -sü nü "gbɩɩ-, kö ꞊ya ö kwaa- ö bha "gbʋnggbʋ ʼö gun- ꞊gwinng- -a -zü "siaa- ; ʼyö pö yöö -sɔ ʼkɔ bha- ʼgü, kö ʼö ö bha ʼnë bha ʼsü, "kɛɛ ʼyö mɛ -nu ʼwo- kun, -a pö -sü ʼka- -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ ʼya ʼdho ö -de zë-. "Kɛɛ yöö- ꞊gban ʼgü, -yö kë ö -kɔ "vlʋʋdɔ -a -nu -gɔ, ʼö dho -dedewo ʼö -sɔ pɛng nɛɛ- bha- ʼgü, ʼö yö ö bha ʼnë bha- ʼka "kpɛnng. Pë ʼbha -bha ʼbha ʼyii kë waa- ö bha ʼnë bha kë tongtongdhö.

ʼWɔn ʼö bha ʼyö mɛ ꞊gban "dhi dɔ bong ʼka.

Dhebë ʼnë bha -yö kë- -zɔn ꞊dhɛ kö mɛ -dhɔ -yö ü kë -dedewo ʼkö ʼzü ü -gɔ ʼö to- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼyaa kë ü ʼgü ʼwɔn ʼbha ʼka.

4. Ziaan ʼö dho ꞊naɔ -bha -yö ꞊gblɛɛn "wɛ -ee ?

ʼNëglɔɔn ʼnë do ʼbha nü ʼsëëbho -dhɛ ꞊kpaɔyi do ʼka, ʼyö- pö -Zlaan -dhɛ ö bha ʼsëë -wo ʼgü : « Atanna -Zlaan, -a kë kö ꞊naɔ -yö nu n -gɔ ʼkɔɔdhö, kö ʼa kë ꞊naɔ -mɛ ʼka -dhe ! » ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -ya bhɛa" bha- wo ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö, ʼö "tϋng kpö ʼnë ʼbha ꞊ya ziö, ʼyö dho "kwi ꞊plöö, ö bha mɛ -nu ꞊tuaabho kë -dhɛ ʼgü. ꞊Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka mü, ʼyö gun ö bha ziaan ziö sië, ʼyö -kpan ꞊gbëë ʼnë sɛɛnnë do "dhi "pu -sü -bha -kpinng -ta kö ʼwëë- "dhɛ -ya pa -sü ʼka "wɛ "sɛnngdhö ꞊dhɛ mɛ -yö -më -kë. ʼYö ʼgbaannu ʼyö ʼwëë- bha- -ga zuudhö. ʼYö -dhɛ -ga ö -züzü, ʼyö ʼyii mɛ ʼbha yö. ʼYö pö yöö ö -kɔ -da ʼgü, "kɛɛ ʼyö ö -zo gɔn, ʼyö- pö ö -de -dhɛ : « ʼWëë- ya ʼa ü ʼsü, "iin ʼa ü kë ʼmü ꞊dhɛ -oo ? A- -pö ꞊tɔn -Zlaan -dhɛ ꞊naɔ -yö nu n -gɔ ʼkɔɔdhö, "kɛɛ -a ʼdhɛ ʼkö ya, -yö -kpinng -ta -wa ! -Kë ꞊dhɛ -wɔn ꞊nɛ -oo ? ʼA ʼdho ü ʼka ꞊tɔn ʼkɔɔdhö -ee ? » ʼYö ö -zo ʼbha gɔn, ʼyö ʼwëë- bha- to ʼyö dho.

꞊Dhɛkpaɔyi "wɛɛ ʼbha ʼka kö ꞊ya ö yeekë ꞊ya ʼdho ʼpödhö, ʼyö gun ꞊niëë sië "ka "flɩɩ- -dhɛ ʼbha ʼö gun ʼpö- "sɔɔ mü, -a ʼgü. ʼÖ dho -dhɛ -ga gwɛ -dhü do ʼbha ʼö gun bha- ꞊wlöö, kö gbɔ ʼkpii- do ʼö- "dhi ʼdhö "pʋ -sü ʼka, -yö mü, kö "sënng -ya pa -sü ʼka "wɛ "sɛnngdhö. ʼYö pö ö -de -dhɛ : « ꞊Naɔ -dede ꞊nɛ, "kɛɛ ʼyaa n -gɔ ꞊tɔn ʼkɔɔdhö -wa n dë -nuu ! »

Kö ꞊ya ʼgbaannu ꞊dhɛ "dhü ʼö ʼwo- gban -a ʼdhö, -ya -ga sië, kö- zuëga -yö ʼzëë- zë kë sië ; kö ʼpë ʼö ziö sië- -gɔ ʼgü ꞊dhɛ -zogɔndhe ʼdhö, -Zlaan nü ö bha pë dɔ. "Kɛɛ ʼyö- to ʼö ö bha ʼdho wo. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ꞊loo "kwanngdhö, ʼyö -kpan ö "tɛɛdo do ʼbha bha, -a -bha, ʼyö- pö- -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ ʼya -kpan "sënng -bha, "kɛɛ -a ʼsü -dhɔ ʼyii kë ö kë. -Yö gbɔ ʼgü gwɛ -dhü ꞊wlöö "ka "flɩɩ- -dhɛ ʼgü. ʼYö- ʼtɔngdë ʼö pö- -dhɛ : « Bhi -zë slaa" nü ü ʼgü. ʼÜ -kpan "sënng -bha ʼyö ʼbhaa- ʼsü ʼkö ꞊dhɛ ? -A "bin ! Ü -ta -yö -ma -sü ʼka -dedewo. »

Dhiang bha -go -a "dhi -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö -ya ziö ꞊dhɛ ꞊saaga -yö -ziö ꞊ya ʼdho mü. -dedewo ʼyö dho ʼyö -kpan gbɔ bha- -bha kö -yö mü "dhϋ tɛan- ʼka, "kɛɛ kö -a -te "dhiϋ -ya "dhiϋ. ʼYö- bho- "dhiϋ. ʼÖ dho -dhɛ -ga kö ꞊mlɛɛ bhɛ -zizisü nü ʼö -ya ö "klϋ kë gbɔ bha- ʼgü ya. ʼYö gbɔ bha- -te "dhiϋ yö- "dhiϋ "lɛɛdhö -deewo, ʼyö dho ʼö "mlüü -kë ʼyö gbɔ bha -a sü "lɛɛdhö ʼö- dɔ ö ꞊gwinng- kö ʼö ʼdho ʼö- -zuö ö "tɔngdë bha- -ta ʼkɔɔdhö. -A -bha ʼgü -a "tɔngdë -yö ꞊sua nü- -kë ö -gɔ ; -a -wɔn ʼgü, ʼyö- "piϋ ꞊dhɛ ʼö ö mlɔɔ bho- -gɔ. ꞊Dhɛ ʼkö ꞊loo ʼkɔ "dhi -bha, ʼö ö "yan -zë -a -kpan ö "tɔngdë bha- -bha ʼkɔɔdhö, dɔ nü ʼö- wo "kpɛnngdhö ʼö gbɔ bha- -zuö -a -ta ʼkɔɔdhö ʼmü kö -ya ziö -biang ʼka ꞊dhɛ ꞊saaga -yö -ziö. Gbɔ bha -a -pö "siaa- -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö ꞊mlɛɛ ʼö gun ʼnu -a ʼgü "dhϋ bha, ꞊ya "gla "sënng ʼgü -deewo ꞊ya ꞊loo "siaa-.

꞊Naɔ -dede ꞊ya nu ꞊tɔn -a -gɔ ʼkɔɔdhö.

꞊Naɔ ʼö gɔndë ʼnë bha ʼö kë- -dhɛ -Zlaan -gɔ bha, -a ʼgü -wɔn -yö kë -kë ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö.

Ö "tϋng ʼö kë- to ö -dega -zë -dhiang ʼgü bha, -a -ga ʼö- ʼgü -wɔn -së ʼö -kë -a -dhɛ bha.

-Yö kë ö zuë" -kë -sɛa ʼgüdandhe -nu bha, -a -nu ʼgü, ʼö -Zlaan dhɔɔbhaa ʼö -kë ꞊dhɛ -kɔ ʼö yöö -dede ʼö kë- pö ʼka -Zlaan -dhɛ bha- ʼdhö.

ʼWɔn yaa ʼö- "tɔngdë ʼö kë- -ya ö zuë" "piϋ ʼö- kë ʼnu- ʼka bha, -yö kë -gla -a -gɔ ʼwɔn -së ʼgü.

Ziaan ʼö dho ꞊naɔ -bha -yö ꞊gblɛɛn. Zuë" -sɛamɛ nü ʼö ꞊mɔɔ- ʼsü -sü -bha, ʼyö- ꞊trɔɔn ꞊slɔɔ.

꞊Ya ʼgo mü, ʼmɛ ʼö ʼbha pö bhii ʼwɔn ʼbha kë, kö ü zuëga -yö ʼzëëzë kö -a kë -sü ʼgü, -yö -së kö ʼbha ʼdho- kë-. -A ʼgbɛ -dhɛ ʼgü ʼyaa dhi mɛ -gɔ. "Kɛɛ ü zuëga -zë ʼyii ʼzëë- zë kë, kö -a kë -sü -yö ü zuë" ꞊niida, -a kë. -A "dhiϋ ta ʼgbɛ -dhɛ -yö -dhi mɛ -gɔ.

5. ꞊Gee do ʼbha -bha dhebë ʼnë do ʼbha ʼkun ʼö- wo ʼnʋbë ʼka

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka, yö ꞊gee ʼö ʼwo- -dhɛ ʼmamɔɔnë, "iin ʼzü "siϋ dhuu" -gee bha ʼö yö "kpɛnng. -A -bha pë -mü "siϋ dhuu" -sü ʼka dhebë -nu -gɔ zuëën- ʼgü, ʼö sü ʼyënng- -kë "gbɩɩ- "tϋng -bha, blɛɛ" yi ʼka ; kë "dhϋ kö "tɛɛ ʼya ʼdho ʼdho- pɛng -klaan -nu ʼka, ʼö ʼwo ʼpö- -gϋ. ꞊Gee bha ꞊ya yö "kpɛnng ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö, ʼyö dhebë -nu ꞊wa ziö- -gɔ -bɛng ʼka. -A -ga, yö ʼö- wo "kpɛnng bha, ʼyö kpa dhebë ʼnë do ʼbha bha- ꞊keng-. Dhebë ʼnë bha, ꞊loo ʼö- wo "wlëëdhɛ ʼbha bha- ʼgü bha, ʼyö- -gɛn ʼdhö -da wöng ʼgü, ʼyö -pö, kö -foo -nu ꞊gban -yaa zë. -Yö -to ʼwaannu -sü ʼka -dhɛ bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ꞊gee bha ʼö nu. Kö ü- -kë mü ꞊dhɛ, ʼbhii -a kë ʼmü ꞊dhɛ -ee, -a -gɛn ʼyii kë -da pë ʼbha ʼgü, "kɛɛ -gblu, yöö ꞊de ʼpö -ya -pö, "kɛɛ dhebë ʼnë bha -a "sɔɔ -dhɛ -dede ʼgü mü. Wɛng -wa -wɔ wo ʼko "dhiϋ mü. -Yö -to dhebë ʼnë "sɔɔ mü ʼyö- pö- -dhɛ : « Mɛ -së, ü -dhɔ ꞊ya n kë "gbɩɩ- -wa. Ü -dhɔ ʼö -bhɔ n kë -sü ʼka, -a yi -ya ꞊gwëë, "kɛɛ maa -a kë ʼnu -kɔ ʼö- ʼgü, ʼmaa gun -a -kɔ yö -sü ʼka. -A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- ʼgü, -yö n "piϋ ꞊dhɛ kwɛng ʼko kë -mlɛɛ ʼgü. Dɔ "gbɩɩ- ʼyɔn -mɛ dhe, n dhɔɔbhaa ».

ʼWɔn bha -yö kë -kë ꞊dhɛ -gwëmɛ -yö ö "yan to wɛngga -gɔ.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö ꞊gee bha ʼö- pö "dhϋ, ʼyö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö- pö : « ʼYö n dë -bha ꞊gee, ʼwɔn ʼkö bha -yö "dhϋ ʼyö ʼbhaa- pö ʼnu n -dhɛ "vaandhö, ʼyö kwɛng ꞊plɛ ʼko sëë "suma bho ya -ee ? ʼYaa "gbɩɩ-, ʼwɔn ʼü- pö bha ʼma- ma. -Siö mɛ -dhɛ -wɔn ʼyaa kë "dhϋ».

ʼKwa- pö "dhϋ, kö kwa- -pö ꞊dhɛ tɛan- -wɔn pö -sü ʼö "vaandhö ʼwɔn -nu ʼgü, wo ʼko nu -dhɛ bha, ʼyö -së. ʼBha ʼdho ü kwaa- ü këyɔɔ -zü ʼö sëëbho kö -blɛɛsü kö ʼü gun -naa tɛan- -wɔn pö- -dhɛ ꞊taama. -A -kë "dhϋ -sü ʼyaa -së.

    
    
    

6. -Kɔ ʼö -kë -a -bha ʼö ʼwo "Maadhɛ -dhɛ "Maadhö

ʼÖ gun "tϋng ʼbha ʼka kö dha ʼyaa ban sië, kö mɛ "bhɩɩ- -nu woo- kë -kɔ ʼö -a -bha kö ʼwo dha "yi ꞊slɔɔ Gbɛɛ" ꞊plöö, kö- -kɔ ʼbhaa ʼdhö.

ʼYö Gbɛɛ" ꞊plöö -mɛ -nu ʼö- -naa "sɛ -yö -kë "Maadhɛ ʼka bha, -a -naa ꞊dhuutii waa- ö dɔ -bha -mɛ -nu, ʼwo dho -dhɛ -ma -ga. ʼÖ gun kë sië "dhϋ bha, kö ʼnë dhebë do nü ꞊dhuutii bha- -gɔ. -A -ga, ʼyö -dɛ ʼdhö- pö ꞊dhɛ ꞊dhuutii bha -yö ö bha ʼnë ga dosɛngsɛng ʼö -a -gɔ bha, -ya kë "saa- ʼka. ꞊Ya bo -kë "dhϋ -sü ʼka dha -yö -dho ban-. "Saa- ʼö "dhϋ bha yö -mü ꞊dhɛ -wo -yɛga do ʼpɔn kö ʼnë ʼö "dhϋ bha, -wa ʼto "bhɩɩ- ʼka kö -wa -zuö ʼgü, -wo "sɛ ꞊loo- -ta. ꞊Dhuutii -kɔ ꞊ya ꞊mɔɔ -a -kë "dhϋ -sü -bha dha -yö -dho ban-, ʼö ta -pë -nu ʼwo -dhi. ʼYö ꞊dhuutii bha ʼö -wɩ -a -bha.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo nu ʼwo ꞊loo wo -yɛɛ ꞊bhaa ʼwii wo "dhi bho- -ta mɛ ʼbha -dhɛ kö ʼyii kë kë ʼpö- dë -nu -kpɛa ʼö ʼwo kë to -a -nu ʼka.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwo dho -gblɛɛn ʼkpɔ ʼgü "bü ꞊zinng ʼgü ʼpö- bha- "sɔɔ, ʼyö -yɛ bha ʼwo- pɔn. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo wo bo, ʼyö ʼwo "kpënng- kpɔ ʼnë bha- -gɔ ʼyö ʼwo dho- ʼka ʼö ʼwo- -ziö -yɛ ga bha ʼgü, ʼwo "sɛ kpa- -ta ꞊dhɛ -kɔ ʼö ʼwo- pö- ʼka -a -nu bha- ʼdhö.

"Saa- bha -a bho -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö dha ʼkpikikpiki -ya -ya ban -sü -bha "siasia- mü.

-A -kë -sü bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ʼwo- pö ꞊dhɛ ʼö -kë ꞊dhɛ ʼnë bha -wo -gun -a -dhɛ sië "Maadhe, ʼö- -gɔ ꞊ya ʼto mɛ ꞊gbaan- ʼwɔn ʼgü bha, -a ʼtɔ bha -wa -ya "Maadhɛ -bha.

ʼPë ʼö -kë ꞊dɛɛ ʼö ʼwo "Maadhɛ -dhɛ "Maadhö bha, ʼyö bha.

-Zlaan -yö -mɔɔ -a -bha ʼö bɔ mɛ doseng -ta ʼö mɛ ʼgbɛ dha, "iin ʼzü ʼö mɛ ʼgbɛ ʼgü ꞊see.

    
    
    

7. ʼMɛʼö ʼyaa ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn "dhiϋ, -ka ka kwaa- -zü kö -a "yan -yö dɔ ʼwɔn ʼgü

"Kwi -gɔ -mɛ ʼkpii- ʼö -kë mɛ tii ʼka, ʼyö- pö yö -zë ʼyaa ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ tongtongdhö. ꞊Ya kë "wɛ, ʼyö -kë -a zë -dhiang ʼka ꞊dhɛ, ʼyaa ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ. ʼMɛ ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya, -yö -gun za -gɔ "yɛ -mɛ nü- ʼka. ꞊Ya kë "kwi -wo ʼgü, ʼyö ʼwo- pö ʼzuzö.

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka, ʼyö gɔndë ʼnë do ʼbha bha ʼö go ö -gɔ ʼpödhö ʼö nu dhebë ʼnë do ʼbha -tazɔn ʼzuzë ꞊plöö dü -wɔn "gblʋʋ "piϋ. ʼWɔn bha -yö kë sië "dhϋ Dannëngdhö. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwo zadɔ -yi -ya -a -nu -gɔ. ꞊Dhɛkpaɔyi bha, mɛ "bhɩɩdhe nu ʼö- wo, -yö -gun -ziisü. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo- -nu dhɛa" kpɔ, ʼyö mɛ -tazɔn -mɛ bha ʼö -ziö ö -wo ʼgü ꞊dhɛ dhebë ʼnë bha nü ö bha ʼnë zë dü ʼgü ; ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö dhe "gbʋʋ- ʼnë bha- dhɛa" kpɔ ʼö- pö : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö, dü -wɔn ʼö ʼwo -ya ü -bha ya -yö "dhϋ tɛan- ʼka -ee ? Tɛan- -mü ꞊dhɛ dü ü -gɔ -ee ? » Dhebë ʼnë bha ʼyii kë- dɔ bhiëë" ꞊gblɛɛn -bha, -a pö nü ʼö- wo ꞊ii. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö- pö "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö- pö- -dhɛ : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö, -a -zɔn mɛ ꞊gban "yaan ʼka yö ꞊dhɛ dü -yö ö -gɔ. »

ʼYö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö- pö -wo yö "kpɛnng. ʼYö mɛ ꞊gban ʼdhö go ʼkɔɔdhö ʼyö ʼwo nu ʼdhuëng- -ta zadɔ ʼgü -kɔ bha- "dhiϋ mü. ʼYö dhe "gbʋʋ- ʼnë bha, ʼö pö -wo ʼdho -tɔ klëën do ʼdhɔ- kö -wo nu- ʼka. "Vaandhö "wɛ ꞊ni, kö ʼpë bha -wa nu- ʼka. ʼYö- pö -wa "dhi kë "bϋwɛ, ʼyö ʼwo- -kë "dhϋ.

Mɛ ꞊gban "pɛpɛ "yan "dhiϋ mü bha, ʼyö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö ö -gɔ -sɔ ʼpë bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö- -dhɛ ꞊gban "pɛpɛ ʼö ma -tɔ klëën bha- ʼgü mü. Kö mɛ ꞊gbaan ꞊wa -ya kwɛɛ" ʼkun -sü -bha. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö pö -wo sɔ kpa ö -ta, ʼyö ʼwo- kpa- -ta. ʼWo dho "kan- wo -ta, kö -tɔ klëën bha, -ya -ya -pa ö diëë -sü -bha. Kö -yö ꞊glüü "glüü kë sië ʼö go- ʼka "siaa-. ʼYö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn bha- "dhiϋ, ʼyö pö : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö -yö ʼto "dhϋ. » ꞊Sua ʼö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö- -kë, -yö -kë ꞊dhɛ mɛ -ya pö ꞊dhaviɛɛyö -bhö ʼdho- -bha ʼbha wo. Pë do ʼö- dɔ -ziaawo -a ʼgü, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-. -Yö -kë ꞊dhɛ "flʋkpongdhe -yö -ziö. -Tɔ klëën waa- dhebë ʼnë ʼö bha ʼdho ʼö ʼwo- ʼwo dhang- ʼgü ʼyi bha -yi bha ʼka, nü ʼö ʼkwa -a -bha dɔ wo ꞊dɛɛ ya. -Waa mɔɔ- -a -gɔ ʼpödhö, -waa mɔɔ- -dhɛ ꞊gban ʼgü, ʼwii -kpan -a -bha ʼö nu ʼö yö- ʼka ꞊dɛɛ -bha.

Za ʼdhɛ ʼö bha -a "dhiϋ -ya -dhɛ -yö kë -kë ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö.

-Yö -sü yi bha nü- -bha, ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ.

ʼMɛ ʼö -yaa pö ʼyaa ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn ʼö "dhiϋ, -ka ʼwɔn -zɔn -a -dhɛ kö- "yan -yö dɔ- ʼgü.

7. ʼMɛʼö ʼyaa ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn "dhiϋ, -ka ka kwaa- -zü kö -a "yan -yö dɔ ʼwɔn ʼgü

"Kwi -gɔ -mɛ ʼkpii- ʼö -kë mɛ tii ʼka, ʼyö- pö yö -zë ʼyaa ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ tongtongdhö. ꞊Ya kë "wɛ, ʼyö -kë -a zë -dhiang ʼka ꞊dhɛ, ʼyaa ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ. ʼMɛ ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya, -yö -gun za -gɔ "yɛ -mɛ nü- ʼka. ꞊Ya kë "kwi -wo ʼgü, ʼyö ʼwo- pö ʼzuzö.

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka, ʼyö gɔndë ʼnë do ʼbha bha ʼö go ö -gɔ ʼpödhö ʼö nu dhebë ʼnë do ʼbha -tazɔn ʼzuzë ꞊plöö dü -wɔn "gblʋʋ "piϋ. ʼWɔn bha -yö kë sië "dhϋ Dannëngdhö. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwo zadɔ -yi -ya -a -nu -gɔ. ꞊Dhɛkpaɔyi bha, mɛ "bhɩɩdhe nu ʼö- wo, -yö -gun -ziisü. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo- -nu dhɛa" kpɔ, ʼyö mɛ -tazɔn -mɛ bha ʼö -ziö ö -wo ʼgü ꞊dhɛ dhebë ʼnë bha nü ö bha ʼnë zë dü ʼgü ; ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö dhe "gbʋʋ- ʼnë bha- dhɛa" kpɔ ʼö- pö : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö, dü -wɔn ʼö ʼwo -ya ü -bha ya -yö "dhϋ tɛan- ʼka -ee ? Tɛan- -mü ꞊dhɛ dü ü -gɔ -ee ? » Dhebë ʼnë bha ʼyii kë- dɔ bhiëë" ꞊gblɛɛn -bha, -a pö nü ʼö- wo ꞊ii. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö- pö "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö- pö- -dhɛ : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö, -a -zɔn mɛ ꞊gban "yaan ʼka yö ꞊dhɛ dü -yö ö -gɔ. »

ʼYö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö- pö -wo yö "kpɛnng. ʼYö mɛ ꞊gban ʼdhö go ʼkɔɔdhö ʼyö ʼwo nu ʼdhuëng- -ta zadɔ ʼgü -kɔ bha- "dhiϋ mü. ʼYö dhe "gbʋʋ- ʼnë bha, ʼö pö -wo ʼdho -tɔ klëën do ʼdhɔ- kö -wo nu- ʼka. "Vaandhö "wɛ ꞊ni, kö ʼpë bha -wa nu- ʼka. ʼYö- pö -wa "dhi kë "bϋwɛ, ʼyö ʼwo- -kë "dhϋ.

Mɛ ꞊gban "pɛpɛ "yan "dhiϋ mü bha, ʼyö dhebë ʼnë bha ʼö ö -gɔ -sɔ ʼpë bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö ö ꞊sɔɔ "sɔɔ -kë, ʼyö- -dhɛ ꞊gban "pɛpɛ ʼö ma -tɔ klëën bha- ʼgü mü. Kö mɛ ꞊gbaan ꞊wa -ya kwɛɛ" ʼkun -sü -bha. ꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö pö -wo sɔ kpa ö -ta, ʼyö ʼwo- kpa- -ta. ʼWo dho "kan- wo -ta, kö -tɔ klëën bha, -ya -ya -pa ö diëë -sü -bha. Kö -yö ꞊glüü "glüü kë sië ʼö go- ʼka "siaa-. ʼYö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn bha- "dhiϋ, ʼyö pö : « ꞊Dhaviɛɛyö -yö ʼto "dhϋ. » ꞊Sua ʼö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö- -kë, -yö -kë ꞊dhɛ mɛ -ya pö ꞊dhaviɛɛyö -bhö ʼdho- -bha ʼbha wo. Pë do ʼö- dɔ -ziaawo -a ʼgü, -yö -gun "gbɩɩ-. -Yö -kë ꞊dhɛ "flʋkpongdhe -yö -ziö. -Tɔ klëën waa- dhebë ʼnë ʼö bha ʼdho ʼö ʼwo- ʼwo dhang- ʼgü ʼyi bha -yi bha ʼka, nü ʼö ʼkwa -a -bha dɔ wo ꞊dɛɛ ya. -Waa mɔɔ- -a -gɔ ʼpödhö, -waa mɔɔ- -dhɛ ꞊gban ʼgü, ʼwii -kpan -a -bha ʼö nu ʼö yö- ʼka ꞊dɛɛ -bha.

Za ʼdhɛ ʼö bha -a "dhiϋ -ya -dhɛ -yö kë -kë ꞊dhɛ -kɔ bha- ʼdhö.

-Yö -sü yi bha nü- -bha, ʼyö ʼzuzö mi bha ʼö ʼdhangbho dü -wɔn "dhiϋ.

ʼMɛ ʼö -yaa pö ʼyaa ʼdhangbho ʼwɔn ʼö "dhiϋ, -ka ʼwɔn -zɔn -a -dhɛ kö- "yan -yö dɔ- ʼgü.

9. ꞊Dhang -bha ꞊dhɛng ʼö- wo ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë do ʼbha ꞊taa, -a gwan ʼkpɔ -yi -dede ʼka

ʼWɔn ʼö ya, ʼwɔn ʼö ꞊ya kë ʼö -ya ꞊mɔɔ dha "yi -kwɛ ʼgbɛ -dede -bha, yö -mü. -Yö -kë "dhϋ ꞊dheglizë ʼö ʼwo- -dhɛ "kwi -wo ʼgü Asangble dö ʼDiö- bha, -a do ʼbha- ʼgü.

ʼYö -gban ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë -tiaandhe do ʼö "tɔngdhe -dhɛ kun ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë ʼö ꞊dhang ʼdhö- ꞊taa -a -bha. ʼNëglɔɔn ʼnë ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya, kpëëʼ -së ʼö gun- -gɔ, ʼa "suma "yɔɔ ʼyaa gun tongtongdhö. ʼYö go ʼmü, ʼyö gun "kwi -yë -tiantiandhe -dede ʼgü. Pë ʼbha -saan ʼyaa gun- -bha. ʼYö- pö ö bha Pasitëë waa- ö ʼkpɔ -mɛ -nu -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë ʼö ꞊dhang ʼdhö- ꞊taa bha nü- -dhɔ ꞊ya ö kë dheglizë bha- ʼgü, ʼnëdhiëng "pɛpɛ ʼö ʼwo mü bha, -a -nu kpö ʼgü. ꞊Dhɛ "dhϋ -wa -za dɔ ö -dhɛ.

-A ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë ꞊de ʼpö -yö -gun -së -dedewo ö wëëʼ dhö ʼö- "suma "yɔɔ ʼyaa gun. -꞊Ya ʼgo mü -a -gɛn "dhü -nu -wo -gun "gblϋgblϋ ʼka, "drɔkɔdrɔkɔ ʼka, -së ʼka ꞊ni.

-A -zë ʼka -dhɛ dosɛng ʼkö gun "wɛ, yö nü gun ꞊dhang bha- ʼka.

ʼWɔn ʼö bha, ʼyö- ʼwɔn ʼdhö mɛ ꞊gban "pɛpɛ kɔn ꞊dheglizë bha- ʼgü. -A ʼkpɔ -mɛ -nu waa- Pasitëë, -waa dhɛa" ʼkpɔ ꞊dhɛ ʼmɛ ʼö- yö ö dhɔɔbhaa ʼka ʼyö bha -ee ? -Ya -pö gbokungbokundhö ö dhɔɔbhaa ʼkö ʼdhö ʼyö bha. -A "tɛɛbë -nu ꞊wa ʼwɔn ꞊gban kë kö -wa -din yën,ʼwii ꞊mɔɔ- -bha. ʼNëdhiëng -kpɛa -nu ʼö ʼwo to, ʼö ꞊yɔɔn mü kö ʼwaa "wɩ -ziaanwo ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha- "piϋ.

ʼÖ ꞊yɔɔn mü, kö ʼmɛ ʼkö -a -naa -Zlaan -wɔn ʼyaa ʼkpakpadhö, kö -wa pö sië ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë bha, ꞊bɛdhɛ nü ʼö -yaa kë ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha- ʼka. ʼYaa "Dhϋ, "wɛɛwɛ ʼyaa kë "dhϋ. Kö mɛ "wɛɛ ʼbha -nu -wa pö sië ꞊dhɛ mɛ ꞊plɛ bha, -a -nu ʼko ʼsü -yi ʼka, ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha, -yö -dho ʼgo- ö -wo -ta, ʼö- pö ʼyaa yöö ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë bha, -a ʼsü ʼzü.

-Wo -to -a ʼka "dhϋ, ʼö- -nu ʼko ʼsü -yi bha ʼö -wo, ʼwo dho mɛɛdhi. Nu -kɔ suu ʼö mɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo- -kë, -a "wɛɛ "suma ʼyii kë ꞊slɔɔ ʼnu do, "iin ʼyii ʼdho ꞊slɔɔ- -a ʼdhɛ ʼkö bha- ziaan -zë ʼgü, dhe ʼsü -wɔn -zë -a "gblʋʋ "piϋ -dhɛ bha- ʼgü. ʼMɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo nu -a -nu -dhɔ -dede -bha, -wo gun mü, ʼyö ʼmɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo nu kö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha, ꞊ya kë- pö -pë ʼka ʼaa bhoo, kö ʼwo ꞊wɛɛ dɔ ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë bha- -bha, ʼwo gun ʼmü ʼpö.

ʼYö ʼMɛɛ- ʼdhɛ ʼö dhe ʼsü -wɔn ʼö -gban -a -bha bha, ʼö mɛ ꞊plɛ bha- -nu dhɛa" kpɔ "ni ʼö- -nu ʼko -dhɔ ʼdhö ʼko -kë, ʼö ʼwo dho ʼto- wo ʼko -gɔ, -a yaa ʼgü, -a -së ʼgü ? ʼYö ʼwo- pö : « ꞊Ii. »

ʼWo gun ʼgo sië mɛɛdhi -kɔ ʼgü, kö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë ʼö bha, -a ʼkpɔ -mɛ -nu -zë "wënng -ya ziö -a -nu wëëdhö, -yö -ga, ʼwɔn -ma -a -nu ʼka -kɔ yaa ʼgü yaa bha, -a -wɔn ʼgü.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö ʼwo go ʼbha, ʼyö ʼwo dho -a -naa ꞊dheglizë ʼgü. ʼYö Pasitëë ʼö gun ʼdhuëë- -kpɔ -a -nu -bha -mɛ ʼka bha, ʼö ꞊yɔɔn ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë bha- "sɔɔ, ʼyö- dhɛa" kpɔ ʼö- pö : « N dhɔɔbhaa, ü -pö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë ʼö ya nü ʼü dho ʼto- -gɔ -ee ? » ʼYö- pö : « ꞊Ii. » -A -pö "dhϋ -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ- kö ʼmɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo nu -a -nu -dhɔ -bha, -wa -ya wo kwɛɛ" ʼkun -sü -bha. Kö -a -san ʼö ʼmɛ -nu ʼö- -nu zë, wo -zë, -wo -suɛɛ nü- ʼsü sië -a ʼka ꞊dhɛ mɛ -yö -më -kë.

꞊Dhɛ Pasitëë -yö ö bo -a -bha ʼka, ʼyö yö gɔɔn- -sü -bha, ʼyö- dhɛa" kpɔ ʼö- pö : « Ma ʼnë, ü- -pö dhebë ʼö ʼbha- yö ü dhɔɔbhaa ʼka, ʼö -kë -a -së ʼgü, ʼö -kë -a yaa ʼgü, ʼö kɛng ʼka dho ʼto ka ʼko "piϋ yö nü ʼö ya -ee ? » ʼYö -dhɛta ʼö dɔ dinngdhö ꞊dhɛ pë -yö dɔ bun ꞊taa -dhɛ ʼgü.

"Wënng ꞊ya ziö mɛ ꞊gban -ya -wo -ma. ʼYö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha ʼö ö "tɔngdhe bha- -ga zuudhö. ʼYö ö "yan -ta -a ʼka, ʼyö- ꞊lɔɔ- ʼka, ʼyö- -da ʼka, ʼyö ꞊lɔɔ- ʼka. ʼYö Pasitëë -ga. ʼYö mɛ -nu -ga ʼdɔɔndhö, ʼyö go ʼmü ʼö ö "tɔngdhe bha- -ga, ʼyö pö "gbɩɩ- ʼka : « ꞊Iiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiii... »

-A -pö "dhϋ -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ-, kö ʼmɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo gun -ya sië -a -nu -san ʼka -wa "kwɛɛ ʼsü "fɔngfɔng ʼka. Bhlɔɔ yaa ʼgü yaa -bha -ma -a dë -nu ʼgü -sü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, kö woo ꞊de ʼpö ꞊wa zun "kpɛnng.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö Pasitëë -ya pö mɛ ꞊plɛ bha- -nu -dhɛ -wo ꞊yɔɔn ö "sɔɔ kö ʼö ʼdhuëë- ʼkpɔ- -nu -bha. ʼYö ʼwo- -kë "dhϋ. ꞊Dhɛ Pasitëë ʼö ʼdhuëë- kpɔ -a -nu -bha "dhϋ "fluudhö, ʼö yöö- "dhiϋ ta -a pö -sü ʼka, ʼaa- -yö kë bha, ʼyö ʼnëdhiëng ʼnë bha, -a -bha ꞊dhang ʼö gun- ꞊taa bha, ʼö ꞊dhɛng ʼgbaandhö, "kɛɛ kö yöö dosɛng nü ʼö gun ꞊dhɛ -a -zë ʼka -dhɛ ʼdhö.

ʼMɛ ʼö ʼka bha, ʼyö ʼwɔn bha ʼö -kë mɛ "bhɩɩ- ʼkɔn -wɔn -së -zë, -a ʼka yi bha- ʼka.

ʼYö- "dhia ʼdhö ma mɛ "pɛpɛ ʼö ʼwo gun -ya ʼka -a -nu -san ʼka bha- ʼgü, ʼyö -kë -gbɛkɛɛdhɛ -së ʼka. ʼYö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë bha, -a -bha -zo -yö -Zlaan -dhɛ -sü -yö mɛ ꞊gban kɔn.

-Zlaan këwɔn -ziizë, -ziizë -yë kë sië -dedewo.

-A -ga, ꞊dhɛ ʼö "tϋng ʼgbɛ -dede ʼö -ziö ʼwɔn ʼdhɛ bha- ziaan ʼgü, ʼyö ʼnëglɔɔn ʼnë "wɛɛ do ʼbha bha ʼyö pö yöö dhe ʼsü. -A "tɔngdhe bha -yö -gun -së -dedewo, "kɛɛ -a "yan ʼyaa gun -dhɛ yö sië. ꞊Dheglizë -gban -bha -nu -wa dhiang zë kö -yö ʼnë "wɛɛ ʼsü, -ya -pö -a "bin ; ö dhɔɔbhaa ʼkö ʼdhö ʼyö bha dosɛng.

꞊Dhɛ ʼö -kë "dhϋ, ʼyö ʼwɔn ʼö ʼkwa ʼgo sië- ma-, ʼö -gban ꞊dhang -mɛ -bha bha, ʼyö ʼmɛ bha ʼyö ma ʼpö, ʼyö -a fɔɔn -yö dɔ ꞊dhɛ -a -bha -yö -mɔɔ -a -bha ʼö -kë "dhϋ ʼpö "kpϋüngdhö.

ʼWo dho mɛɛdhi, ʼwo go ʼmü, ʼwo nu ꞊dheglizë ʼgü, ʼö Pasitëë ʼö -naa bhɛa" wo, ʼwɔn ʼbha ʼyii kë ʼgü tongtongdhö ʼö nu ʼö zun- ʼka ꞊dɛɛ -bha.

ʼKwa ʼdho- pö kwa -de -dhɛ, ꞊dhɛ ʼö -kë ꞊dhɛ -Zlaan ꞊ya ʼwɔn ʼdhɛ ʼö ya -a kë kwa "këyɔɔ -dhɛ, kwaa kwa -bha kë ʼpö ꞊dhɛ -a -bha ʼdhö, kö -Zlaan -yö nu kwa -dhɛ ꞊dhɛ -a -bha ʼdhö. -Kwa kwa -de ʼkun.

10. -Dhidhawɔn ʼkpii- do ʼö -gban -wëëmɛ do -bha ꞊naɔɔ ꞊slɔɔ -sü –bha

-Dhɛkpaɔyi do ʼka ʼDannëng "sɛ ʼgü, ʼpödhɛ do ʼbha bha- ʼgü, ʼyö -wëëmɛ do ʼbha bha ʼö ö "yɛɛn bho gbeng do ʼgü. Gɔndë ʼnë ʼö ʼkwa "wɩ sië- ʼka ya nü ʼö gun "flɛɛmɛ -nu ꞊gban "dhiϋ ʼto -dhɛ ʼka ʼpö- bha- ʼgü. -A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- ʼgü, ʼö ꞊yɔɔn mü kö -kɔ -ya "kan- "dhiϋ, kö -ya kë "yɛɛn -to -bha -mɛ nü- ʼka, kö- -dhɔ ʼyaa mɛ ʼbha kë ʼzü -a -bha "flɛɛdhɛ -wɔn ʼgü, "kɛɛ kö ʼyii kë- "dhiϋ wlüü" -a -bha ʼsa.

Ö "yɛɛn ʼö- bho "dhϋ bha, ʼyö -Zlaan -ya pö -dhɛ -yö -dho ꞊naɔ ꞊slɔɔ-, "kɛɛ "sanni -yö kë "dhϋ, -a -dhɛ -ya -bha kö ʼpö- bha- ʼgü -mɛ -nu : ʼnë "piϋ, dhe "piϋ, gɔɔn- "piϋ, mɛ ꞊gban -wo ꞊wɔɔ "wɩ -kɔ pö. -Wa pö : « -Kiaankuun. » ꞊Ya kë -dedewo ꞊dhɛ -waa pö "dhϋ, -yö -dho kë- ꞊naɔ -mɛ ʼö- -wɔn pö bha- ʼka. ʼWɔn bha -yö -gun -a -gɔ ʼwɔn "gbɩɩ- ʼka. ʼMɛ ʼö- -dhɔ ʼyaa mɛ ʼbha kë de ʼö dho ö "tʋ to -a -mɛ -wo -bha ?

"Kɛɛ yöö- ꞊gban ʼgü, ꞊dhɛ ʼkö -dhɛ -zë ʼö ꞊kpaɔ, -da nü ʼö gɔndë ʼnë bha, ʼö- wo ʼpö- "piϋ, -dhɛɛ "dhiϋ bho -sü ʼka ʼö- pö : « Mɛ "pɛpɛ ʼö ʼka ʼpö- ya- ʼgüü, ʼnë "piϋ, dhe "piϋ, gɔɔn- "piϋ, -kwa ʼflüü-. -Ka n gba ka "tʋ ʼka -së ʼkaa. N dë -nu, n dhe -nu, ma ʼnë -nu. -Zlaan -yö kë dhiang -zë n -dhɛ gbeng "yɛɛn -wo ʼgüü. -Ya -pö n -dhɛ a -dho ʼgo- "flɛɛdhɛ ʼgü, ʼa -kë ꞊naɔ -mɛ -dede ʼkaa. "Kɛɛ "sanni ʼa kë- ʼka, ʼmɛ ʼö "dhϋ ʼdodo kwa -gɔ ʼpö- ya- ʼgü, -ya pö -kiaankuun... Kö ʼdhuëë- -yö ka ʼkun -a ma -sü ziaan ʼgü bha, ʼaa -yö këë ? »

ʼAA ʼwɔn bha -a -pö "dhϋ -sü nü ʼö "gbɩɩ-, kö mɛ ꞊gbaan -ya "yɩɩ ʼto -sü -bha. Mɛ ʼbha -nu -waa "yɩɩ ʼto -yö -kë ꞊dhɛ -a -nu ko yöö "yɛ- -ta. ʼMɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo -kë ꞊dhɛ ʼwɔn dɔ -mɛ -nu ʼdhö, kö -wa pö sië slaa" -dee "dhiϋ bha. Gɔndë ʼnë -san -bha -a -nu zë -sü yaa ʼgü yaa bha- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼmɛ ʼbha ꞊ya dɔ ʼyö ʼpö : « ʼMaa n -de ꞊bhlëë nü ʼö- dɔ, ʼyö maa- pö : -kiaankuu. »

Mɛ "wɛɛ ʼbha ꞊ya dɔ ʼyö- pö : « Yë nü ʼyaa n -bha ʼyö maa- pö -kiaankuun. »

ʼNë ʼsɛɛnnë -nu -zë -a -nu dhɔɔbhaa -wɔn -nu nü ʼö ʼwo bha. ʼÖ ꞊yɔɔn mü, ꞊wa dɔ gɔndë ʼnë -a "yan "dhiϋ, mɛ ʼbha -yaa pö -kiaankuun, ʼyö mɛ "wɛɛ ʼbha ʼdhö- "dhiϋ kun -kiaankuun, ʼyö -waa "yɩɩ ʼto klee" klee" dhö -wa ziö- ʼka.

Mɛ "gblϋgblϋ ʼbha -nu ʼö ʼwo -kë zuë" "dhiϋϋ- -mɛ -nu, "dhi -dhɛ yaa- -mɛ -nu ʼka, ʼyö ʼwo -ziö ʼwo dho gɔndë ʼnë bha- -gɔ "kwanngdhö, ʼwo -ya -a "yan ʼgü, ʼwo- pö- -dhɛ : « -Dhɛ -ga ! Slaa" ʼö yöö ü kë ʼü "wɩ sië -kiaankuun ꞊dhɛ ꞊wɔɔ -yö -wɩ bha, ʼbhii- "dhiϋ ʼto, ü -go ʼpö- ya- ʼgü -sü -mü. » -A -nu -zo ʼyaa- ʼka ꞊dhɛ -a pö -dede nü ʼö ʼwo- wo sië bha. ʼMɛ -nu ʼö ʼwo go ʼpödhö ʼö ʼwo dho dhɛngdhö, ʼyö ʼwo dho saanwo ʼdhɛ bha- ʼka.

-Wo -dho -a ʼka "dhϋ ʼdodo, ʼö- -nu ꞊gban ʼwo- pö. -Dhɛkpaɔyi -yö -kë -zlëëdhö, ʼyö ʼmɛ bha ʼö -kë ꞊naɔ -mɛ "mlümlüsü ʼka ʼpö- bha- ʼgü, ꞊dhɛ -kɔ ʼö -Zlaan -yö kë- pö- ʼka- -dhɛ bha- ʼdhö. ʼÖ dɔ mü kö- ʼgü -ya kë "gbɩɩ-.

ʼWɔn ʼdhɛ ʼö ʼyii kë "wɩ- -bha ʼpö- kö bha- ʼgü, mɛ ʼbha ʼyaa- kë.

-Kwaa kë -së kö -wëëmɛ -nu -san ʼya ʼdho- pö ʼö kwa zë "wɛɛwɛ kö- -gɛn ʼyaa ʼdhö. ʼKwaa "dhiëng "dhiϋ dhö dɔ kwa -de -gɔ. ʼMɛ ʼö- -san ʼö ʼkwa zë kö -gɛn ʼyaa ʼdhö bha, ʼkwii- kë -së, ʼyiöö- -yö -dho dɔ kwa -bha -a wëëdhö.

11. ʼGbiöödhe do waa- -gblünng ꞊gɔɔn ʼö ʼwo- wo

Yi do ʼka, "sɛ ʼö ʼwo- -Mɔɔsii "sɛ -kë bha- ʼgü, ʼpödhɛ do ʼbha ʼgü, ʼyö ʼgbiöödhe do ʼbha ʼö- ʼgu ꞊ya gun ꞊ya bhɔ -dedewo bha, ʼö dho "bhlaa-. -A ʼdho -sü ʼka, ʼyö -a -bha ʼnë ʼnë ʼö gun- -kɔ "piϋ waa- -bha ʼgbɛn- ʼnë ʼö gun- -gɔ, wɛng- -nu ʼwo dho. ʼYënng- ʼbhü -kɔ yaa ʼgü yaa ʼö "sɛ bha- ʼgü bha- -wɔn ʼgü, ʼyö sɔ kpɔ dhɔng -dhɛ "dhü ꞊wlöö, ʼyö ʼnë bha- -wɔ -a -ta, ʼyö ʼgbɛn- ʼnë bha to- "sɔɔ mü, ʼyö yö -zë ʼö dho ö bha yë kë -dhɛ ʼgü. -A -dhɛ -yö -wɔ -zlëëdhö, ʼyö ʼgbɛn- ʼnë bha ʼö -ya "wɩ -sü -bha, "kɛɛ ʼyii kë- ʼgü ʼwɔn ʼbha ʼka ; ʼyö- bho ö "tʋʋ. ʼÖ ꞊yɔɔ mü -yaa bho ö "tʋʋ "wɛ, ee-. ʼGbɛn- bha "wɩ nü ʼö- bho sië "dhϋ do ʼö dho- ʼka.

-A -kë "dhϋ -sü bha- ʼgü, ʼyö ö ꞊kwaa yë kë -sü -zü ʼyö nu ö mɔɔʼ bho -dhɛ ʼgü. ʼÖ dho -dhɛ -ga, kö -gblünng bhɛ -zizisü nü ʼö na kë sië ʼnë bha- -bha kö ʼö- "mëng ya. Yöö- kë ʼmü ꞊dhɛ ? "Bang ʼö gun- -gɔ, -a ʼgü ʼyaa ʼdhö.
